L000333|# MACHINE_READABLE_CONTROL_PRINCIPLES
L000334|CONTROL_RECORD|ID=CP001|TEXT=Source gives the material. Author chooses the vessel. Editorial makes the vessel receivable. Reader completes the field.
L000335|CONTROL_RECORD|ID=CP002|TEXT=Form is the vessel. Image is the carrier. Rhythm is the breath. Structure is the path. Voice is the presence. Editing is the discipline.
L000336|CONTROL_RECORD|ID=CP003|TEXT=Write until the source appears. Edit until the vessel can carry it.
L000337|CONTROL_RECORD|ID=CP004|TEXT=The source may be infinite, but the vessel must be finite.
L000338|CONTROL_RECORD|ID=CP005|TEXT=Do not only ask whether the piece works. Ask which carrier is overloaded and which condition has not yet appeared.
L000339|# END_MACHINE_READABLE_CONTROL_PRINCIPLES

L000400|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC01|ORIGINAL_LINE=0057|RAW=L0057|ITEM|ID=S01.001|NAME=Haiku|CLASS=form|USE=Extreme compression; image, season, moment, turn; often 5/7/5 in English practice, though not mandatory in Japanese tradition.
L000401|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC01|ORIGINAL_LINE=0058|RAW=L0058|ITEM|ID=S01.002|NAME=Tanka|CLASS=form|USE=Short lyric expansion beyond haiku; often 5/7/5/7/7; turns from image into feeling.
L000402|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC01|ORIGINAL_LINE=0059|RAW=L0059|ITEM|ID=S01.003|NAME=Senryu|CLASS=form|USE=Haiku-like compression focused on human nature, irony, behavior, and social observation.
L000403|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC01|ORIGINAL_LINE=0060|RAW=L0060|ITEM|ID=S01.004|NAME=Sonnet|CLASS=form|USE=Fourteen-line argument or emotional pressure vessel; often includes a volta.
L000404|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC01|ORIGINAL_LINE=0061|RAW=L0061|ITEM|ID=S01.005|NAME=Villanelle|CLASS=form|USE=Repetition, obsession, circular return; fixed refrains generate inevitability.
L000405|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC01|ORIGINAL_LINE=0062|RAW=L0062|ITEM|ID=S01.006|NAME=Pantoum|CLASS=form|USE=Repeating-line structure for memory, recursion, echo, and altered return.
L000406|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC01|ORIGINAL_LINE=0063|RAW=L0063|ITEM|ID=S01.007|NAME=Ghazal|CLASS=form|USE=Autonomous couplets held by refrain/rhyme; longing, separation, mystical intensity.
L000407|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC01|ORIGINAL_LINE=0064|RAW=L0064|ITEM|ID=S01.008|NAME=Ode|CLASS=form|USE=Praise, elevation, address, devotion, attention to an object or force.
L000408|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC01|ORIGINAL_LINE=0065|RAW=L0065|ITEM|ID=S01.009|NAME=Elegy|CLASS=form|USE=Grief, mourning, remembrance, lament, and transformation after loss.
L000409|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC01|ORIGINAL_LINE=0066|RAW=L0066|ITEM|ID=S01.010|NAME=Epigram|CLASS=form|USE=Sharp compressed wit or insight; a small blade of thought.

L000883|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0040|RAW=### 0.1 Known from direct notes and reflections
L000884|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0041|RAW=
L000885|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0042|RAW=The event was recorded in notes as an author conversation organized by the **Royal Literary Fund**. The named roles from the thread/reflection were:
L000886|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0043|RAW=
L000887|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0044|RAW=| Role | Person / source as recorded | Status |
L000888|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0045|RAW=|---|---|---|
L000889|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0046|RAW=| Chair / conversation guide | Leila / Layla Rasheed | Name/spelling to confirm if needed |
L000890|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0047|RAW=| Fiction/editorial/collaborative-writing author | Meg / Meg Sanders | Name/spelling to confirm if needed |
L000891|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0048|RAW=| Poet / discipline / maker-craft angle | Michael Woods / Michael Wood | Name/spelling to confirm if needed |
L000892|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0049|RAW=| Referenced reading / example | Catherine Stansfield, including a piece called *A Day in the Life of a Writer* | Title/person from notes; not externally checked here |
L000893|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0050|RAW=
L000894|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0051|RAW=The notes record that the event covered:
L000895|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0052|RAW=
L000896|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0053|RAW=- day-to-day writing discipline;
L000897|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0054|RAW=- professional routes into writing;
L000898|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0055|RAW=- poetry, fiction, editing, collaboration, co-authoring;
L000899|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0056|RAW=- agents and publishing routes;
L000900|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0057|RAW=- editing and cutting dense material;
L000901|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0058|RAW=- theme, metaphor, image, and structure as carriers of meaning;
L000902|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0059|RAW=- writing as emotional channeling;
L000903|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0060|RAW=- the shift from “I” to “it” when a piece becomes its own object;
L000904|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0061|RAW=- the professional reality that writers often do multiple things, not only one thing.
L000905|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0062|RAW=
L000906|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0063|RAW=### 0.2 Inferred lessons
L000907|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0064|RAW=
L000908|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0065|RAW=The event appears to answer a live personal problem: how to take dense, meaning-heavy Source material and make it legible, publishable, and usable without flattening it.
L000909|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0066|RAW=
L000910|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0067|RAW=The primary inference:
L000911|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0068|RAW=
L000912|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0069|RAW=> **The issue is not that the source carries too much meaning. The issue is that too much meaning is trying to pass through the same carrier at once.**
L000913|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0070|RAW=
L000914|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0071|RAW=The editorial solution is to distribute meaning across words, form, image, theme, metaphor, structure, silence, rhythm, and reader participation.
L000915|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0072|RAW=
L000916|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0073|RAW=### 0.3 Not verified here
L000917|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0074|RAW=
L000918|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0075|RAW=This file does **not** verify:
L000919|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0076|RAW=
L000920|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0077|RAW=- exact bibliographies;
L000921|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0078|RAW=- exact publication counts;
L000922|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0079|RAW=- exact author biographies;
L000923|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0080|RAW=- exact titles beyond what was recorded in notes;
L000924|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0081|RAW=- external professional income streams for each author;
L000925|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0082|RAW=- whether every phrase remembered was said verbatim.
L000926|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0083|RAW=
L000927|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0084|RAW=This file preserves lessons and operating patterns from the event, not external literary scholarship.
L000928|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0085|RAW=
L000929|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0086|RAW=---
L000930|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0087|RAW=
L000931|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0088|RAW=# 1. Executive synthesis
L000932|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0089|RAW=
L000933|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0090|RAW=## 1.1 Core lesson
L000934|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0091|RAW=
L000935|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0092|RAW=When a piece carries too much meaning, the task is not to weaken the meaning. The task is to decide which carrier holds which part of the meaning.
L000936|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0093|RAW=
L000937|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0094|RAW=Meaning can be carried by:
L000938|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0095|RAW=
L000939|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0096|RAW=| Carrier | Function |
L000940|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0097|RAW=|---|---|
L000941|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0098|RAW=| Words | Say the explicit message |
L000942|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0099|RAW=| Structure | Orders the reader’s experience |
L000943|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0100|RAW=| Image | Lets the reader feel meaning without explanation |
L000944|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0101|RAW=| Theme | Holds continuity across the piece |
L000945|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0102|RAW=| Metaphor | Carries depth without over-explaining |
L000946|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0103|RAW=| Form | Creates pressure, proportion, and limitation |
L000947|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0104|RAW=| Silence / omission | Gives the reader space to complete the meaning |
L000948|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0105|RAW=| Rhythm | Controls emotional pacing |
L000949|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0106|RAW=| Juxtaposition | Lets meaning appear through contrast |
L000950|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0107|RAW=| Reader participation | Allows the work to live beyond authorial control |
L000951|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0108|RAW=
L000952|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0109|RAW=So the editorial task is not “cut the truth down.”
L000953|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0110|RAW=
L000954|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0111|RAW=It is:
L000955|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0112|RAW=
L000956|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0113|RAW=> **Cut the overload so the truth can travel.**
L000957|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0114|RAW=
L000958|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0115|RAW=## 1.2 The main correction
L000959|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0116|RAW=
L000960|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0117|RAW=Do not ask:
L000961|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0118|RAW=
L000962|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0119|RAW=> “How do I fit all the meaning in?”
L000963|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0120|RAW=
L000964|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0121|RAW=Ask:
L000965|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0122|RAW=
L000966|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0123|RAW=> **“What is the smallest vessel that still carries the living charge?”**
L000967|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0124|RAW=
L000968|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0125|RAW=Compression is not loss. Compression is incarnation.
L000969|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0126|RAW=
L000970|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0127|RAW=The unmanifested becomes real not when everything is included, but when the right form can hold enough of it to move another person.
L000971|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0128|RAW=
L000972|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0129|RAW=---
L000973|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0130|RAW=
L000974|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0131|RAW=# 2. Event map
L000975|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0132|RAW=
L000976|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0133|RAW=## 2.1 The event as a three-function model
L000977|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0134|RAW=
L000978|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0135|RAW=The event can be read as three live functions in one room:
L000979|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0136|RAW=
L000980|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0137|RAW=| Function | Person / role | What they represented | Lesson for the work |
L000981|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0138|RAW=|---|---|---|---|
L000982|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0139|RAW=| Editorial / collaborative author function | Meg | Editing, fiction, collaboration, deadlines, agents, professional routes | The work needs externalization, deadlines, and an editorial cut that protects legibility |
L000983|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0140|RAW=| Poet / maker function | Michael | Discipline, form, emotion, haiku/sonnet scale, small vessels | The charge needs form-pressure; the form does not weaken the source, it makes it transmissible |
L000984|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0141|RAW=| Chair / guiding question function | Leila / Layla | Conversation structure, question-led unfolding, day-to-day writer life | A good question can govern the field and prevent the discussion or manuscript from sprawling |
L000985|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0142|RAW=
L000986|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0143|RAW=## 2.2 The fourth presence: the referenced text
L000987|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0144|RAW=
L000988|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0145|RAW=Catherine Stansfield’s *A Day in the Life of a Writer*, as recorded in the notes, served as a form example.
L000989|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0146|RAW=
L000990|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0147|RAW=The specific lesson taken from it:
L000991|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0148|RAW=
L000992|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0149|RAW=> **Spread-out juxtaposition can hold ordinary life, interior movement, and unusual structure at once.**
L000993|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0150|RAW=
L000994|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0151|RAW=This matters because it shows that writing does not have to become linear explanation to be legible. It can remain spatial, patterned, fragmentary, and still professional if the form is deliberate.
L000995|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0152|RAW=
L000996|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0153|RAW=---
L000997|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0154|RAW=
L000998|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0155|RAW=# 3. The question asked at the event
L000999|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0156|RAW=
L001000|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0157|RAW=## 3.1 Original question shape
L001001|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0158|RAW=
L001002|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0159|RAW=The live question asked was essentially:
L001003|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0160|RAW=
L001004|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0161|RAW=> When a message carries a lot of meaning, how do you decide what to cut from the language, how much to carry through the structure, and how much to carry through the image?
L001005|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0162|RAW=
L001006|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0163|RAW=This is a highly accurate question for the current writing problem.
L001007|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0164|RAW=
L001008|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0165|RAW=It separates three meaning-carriers:
L001009|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0166|RAW=
L001010|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0167|RAW=| Layer | Question |
L001011|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0168|RAW=|---|---|
L001012|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0169|RAW=| Language | What must be said directly? |
L001013|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0170|RAW=| Structure | What must be experienced through order, sequence, spacing, and architecture? |
L001014|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0171|RAW=| Image | What must be perceived, felt, or intuited without explanation? |
L001015|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0172|RAW=
L001016|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0173|RAW=## 3.2 Answer received
L001017|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0174|RAW=
L001018|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0175|RAW=The answer, as understood through the reflections:
L001019|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0176|RAW=
L001020|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0177|RAW=- it is an editorial issue;
L001021|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0178|RAW=- write the big piece first;
L001022|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0179|RAW=- get the material out;
L001023|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0180|RAW=- then cut down according to essence;
L001024|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0181|RAW=- some pieces may lose a quarter;
L001025|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0182|RAW=- some may lose three quarters;
L001026|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0183|RAW=- sometimes less is more;
L001027|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0184|RAW=- the goal is to bring the work down to the essence;
L001028|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0185|RAW=- theme and metaphor can carry the heavy load;
L001029|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0186|RAW=- the writer intends, but the reader also completes the meaning.
L001030|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0187|RAW=
L001031|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0188|RAW=## 3.3 Practical conclusion
L001032|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0189|RAW=
L001033|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0190|RAW=The large manuscript is not the final work. It is the extraction field.
L001034|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0191|RAW=
L001035|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0192|RAW=> **The 23-page source is the quarry. The 1–3 page manuscript is the cut stone.**
L001036|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0193|RAW=
L001037|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0194|RAW=---
L001038|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0195|RAW=
L001039|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0196|RAW=# 4. What each person gave
L001040|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0197|RAW=
L001041|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0198|RAW=## 4.1 Meg — editorial intelligence, collaboration, professional plurality
L001042|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0199|RAW=
L001043|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0200|RAW=### Main lessons
L001044|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0201|RAW=
L001045|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0202|RAW=Meg’s contribution, as captured in the notes, revolved around:
L001046|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0203|RAW=
L001047|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0204|RAW=- writing, thinking, and speaking about writing from many angles;
L001048|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0205|RAW=- fiction needing deadlines;
L001049|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0206|RAW=- collaboration and co-authoring;
L001050|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0207|RAW=- one person writing one character while another carries another character;
L001051|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0208|RAW=- making internal thinking explicit to the person you work with;
L001052|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0209|RAW=- “what-iffing” / blue-skying / brainstorming;
L001053|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0210|RAW=- devices of plot;
L001054|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0211|RAW=- editorial routes and agents;
L001055|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0212|RAW=- the need for editors in fiction;
L001056|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0213|RAW=- professional routes that involve multiple kinds of work, not one narrow identity.
L001057|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0214|RAW=
L001058|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0215|RAW=### Translation for the work
L001059|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0216|RAW=
L001060|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0217|RAW=Meg points toward the **externalization function**.
L001061|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0218|RAW=
L001062|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0219|RAW=The source field may be vast internally, but collaboration requires making enough of the hidden architecture explicit that another person can continue the relay.
L001063|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0220|RAW=
L001064|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0221|RAW=Key sentence:
L001065|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0222|RAW=
L001066|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0223|RAW=> **If the work is going to collaborate with an editor, reader, model, publisher, or audience, the hidden structure has to become shareable.**
L001067|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0224|RAW=
L001068|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0225|RAW=### Applied principle
L001069|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0226|RAW=
L001070|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0227|RAW=| Meg lesson | Application |
L001071|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0228|RAW=|---|---|
L001072|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0229|RAW=| Fiction needs deadline | Put writing into bounded delivery windows |
L001073|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0230|RAW=| Collaboration requires explicitness | Make the inner map readable to another mind |
L001074|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0231|RAW=| Co-authoring works like relay | Treat each draft as a baton pass, not a final self-definition |
L001075|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0232|RAW=| Agent/editor route matters | Professional writing is ecosystem work, not only expression |
L001076|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0233|RAW=| New discipline can aid explanation | Being new to a field can help write for other newcomers |
L001077|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0234|RAW=
L001078|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0235|RAW=### Professional-author lesson from Meg
L001079|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0236|RAW=
L001080|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0237|RAW=Professional authors often do not rely on one output type. They may write, edit, co-author, teach, speak, advise, collaborate, publish, and appear at events.
L001081|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0238|RAW=
L001082|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0239|RAW=For the Source Voice trajectory, this means:
L001083|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0240|RAW=
L001084|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0241|RAW=> **Do not reduce the writing path to one book. Build a language ecosystem.**
L001085|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0242|RAW=
L001086|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0243|RAW=---
L001087|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0244|RAW=
L001088|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0245|RAW=## 4.2 Michael — maker-craft, discipline, emotion, form-pressure
L001089|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0246|RAW=
L001090|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0247|RAW=### Main lessons
L001091|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0248|RAW=
L001092|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0249|RAW=Michael’s contribution, as captured in the notes, revolved around:
L001093|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0250|RAW=
L001094|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0251|RAW=- poet as “maker”;
L001095|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0252|RAW=- writing as discipline and panic;
L001096|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0253|RAW=- emotional channeling;
L001097|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0254|RAW=- haiku and sonnets;
L001098|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0255|RAW=- small forms carrying large charge;
L001099|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0256|RAW=- poems distributed through small physical/public artifacts;
L001100|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0257|RAW=- craft and trade: learn what is well made;
L001101|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0258|RAW=- the writer’s intent meeting the reader’s interpretation.
L001102|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0259|RAW=
L001103|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0260|RAW=### Translation for the work
L001104|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0261|RAW=
L001105|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0262|RAW=Michael points toward the **form-pressure function**.
L001106|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0263|RAW=
L001107|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0264|RAW=The source can be intense, but intensity must be given a vessel. Form is not the enemy of source. Form is the container that lets source survive contact with a reader.
L001108|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0265|RAW=
L001109|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0266|RAW=Key sentence:
L001110|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0267|RAW=
L001111|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0268|RAW=> **The charge does not become weaker when it enters form. It becomes available.**
L001112|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0269|RAW=
L001113|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0270|RAW=### Applied principle
L001114|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0271|RAW=
L001115|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0272|RAW=| Michael lesson | Application |
L001116|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0273|RAW=|---|---|
L001117|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0274|RAW=| Poet = maker | Treat writing as making, not only channeling |
L001118|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0275|RAW=| Discipline and panic | Use pressure without becoming governed by panic |
L001119|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0276|RAW=| Emotion is fuel | Transform raw charge into crafted form |
L001120|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0277|RAW=| Haiku/sonnet/form | Use constraint to concentrate meaning |
L001121|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0278|RAW=| Small public artifacts | Let small vessels carry large signals |
L001122|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0279|RAW=| Reader completes meaning | Stop trying to control all interpretation through over-explanation |
L001123|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0280|RAW=
L001124|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0281|RAW=### Professional-author lesson from Michael
L001125|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0282|RAW=
L001126|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0283|RAW=A writer can distribute work across small formats, readings, teaching, craft, public surfaces, poems, events, competitions, and publications.
L001127|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0284|RAW=
L001128|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0285|RAW=For the Source Voice trajectory, this means:
L001129|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0286|RAW=
L001130|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0287|RAW=> **The work can exist at multiple scales: line, fragment, note, poem, essay, manuscript, talk, diagnostic, public artifact.**
L001131|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0288|RAW=
L001132|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0289|RAW=---
L001133|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0290|RAW=
L001134|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0291|RAW=## 4.3 Leila / Layla — chairing, question governance, field guidance
L001135|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0292|RAW=
L001136|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0293|RAW=### Main lessons
L001137|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0294|RAW=
L001138|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0295|RAW=The chair’s function was to guide the authors through the conversation, especially around the day-to-day life of a writer.
L001139|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0296|RAW=
L001140|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0297|RAW=The chair does not need to be the loudest voice. The chair creates the field in which the right material can surface.
L001141|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0298|RAW=
L001142|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0299|RAW=### Translation for the work
L001143|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0300|RAW=
L001144|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0301|RAW=This points toward the **chairing principle**.
L001145|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0302|RAW=
L001146|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0303|RAW=A manuscript needs a chair. A conversation with source needs a chair. A writing session needs a chair.
L001147|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0304|RAW=
L001148|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0305|RAW=The chairing principle is the governing question that keeps the piece from becoming everything at once.
L001149|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0306|RAW=
L001150|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0307|RAW=Examples:
L001151|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0308|RAW=
L001152|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0309|RAW=| Piece type | Chairing question |
L001153|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0310|RAW=|---|---|
L001154|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0311|RAW=| Source manuscript | What is trying to come through? |
L001155|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0312|RAW=| Reader-facing essay | What is the one thing the reader must receive? |
L001156|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0313|RAW=| Poem | What image carries the charge? |
L001157|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0314|RAW=| Diagnostic | What is the pressure point? |
L001158|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0315|RAW=| Book chapter | What movement must this chapter complete? |
L001159|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0316|RAW=| Instagram/story post | What can land in one glance? |
L001160|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0317|RAW=
L001161|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0318|RAW=### Core principle
L001162|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0319|RAW=
L001163|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0320|RAW=> **Without a chairing question, source sprawls. With a chairing question, source becomes a field.**
L001164|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0321|RAW=
L001165|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0322|RAW=---
L001166|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0323|RAW=
L001167|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0324|RAW=# 5. Core writing principles extracted
L001168|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0325|RAW=
L001169|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0326|RAW=## 5.1 Big piece first, essence second
L001170|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0327|RAW=
L001171|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0328|RAW=The first draft can be excessive. It can ramble. It can carry too much. That is not failure. That is excavation.
L001172|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0329|RAW=
L001173|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0330|RAW=The large source text is the extraction layer.
L001174|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0331|RAW=
L001175|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0332|RAW=The second task is not to keep everything. The second task is to find the living center.
L001176|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0333|RAW=
L001177|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0334|RAW=### Operating rule
L001178|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0335|RAW=
L001179|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0336|RAW=| Phase | Permission | Discipline |
L001180|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0337|RAW=|---|---|---|
L001181|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0338|RAW=| Source draft | Allow excess | Do not judge too early |
L001182|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0339|RAW=| Essence pass | Identify contribution | Separate signal from overflow |
L001183|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0340|RAW=| Editorial pass | Cut for life | Remove congestion, not charge |
L001184|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0341|RAW=| Reader pass | Test entry | Make the work enterable |
L001185|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0342|RAW=
L001186|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0343|RAW=## 5.2 Central plot of contribution
L001187|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0344|RAW=
L001188|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0345|RAW=The event produced the phrase/idea:
L001189|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0346|RAW=
L001190|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0347|RAW=> **central plot of contribution**
L001191|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0348|RAW=
L001192|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0349|RAW=This means the aim of the writing: what the piece is actually giving.
L001193|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0350|RAW=
L001194|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0351|RAW=Do not ask only:
L001195|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0352|RAW=
L001196|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0353|RAW=- What does this contain?
L001197|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0354|RAW=- What does this mean to me?
L001198|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0355|RAW=- What is hidden inside it?
L001199|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0356|RAW=
L001200|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0357|RAW=Ask:
L001201|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0358|RAW=
L001202|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0359|RAW=- What does this piece contribute?
L001203|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0360|RAW=- What can the reader take from it?
L001204|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0361|RAW=- What transformation does it invite?
L001205|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0362|RAW=- What does it make more visible?
L001206|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0363|RAW=
L001207|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0364|RAW=## 5.3 From “I” to “it”
L001208|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0365|RAW=
L001209|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0366|RAW=At first the work is “I.”
L001210|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0367|RAW=
L001211|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0368|RAW=Then it becomes “it.”
L001212|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0369|RAW=
L001213|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0370|RAW=Once the poem, story, essay, or manuscript has its own life, the author can stop defending every sentence as self-expression. The work becomes an object that can be shaped.
L001214|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0371|RAW=
L001215|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0372|RAW=### Applied transformation
L001216|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0373|RAW=
L001217|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0374|RAW=| Stage | Relationship to work | Editing risk | Required move |
L001218|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0375|RAW=|---|---|---|---|
L001219|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0376|RAW=| I-stage | The work feels like self | Cutting feels like self-harm | Let the draft exist without finalizing it |
L001220|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0377|RAW=| It-stage | The work has its own life | Over-editing can flatten it | Shape the object for its own integrity |
L001221|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0378|RAW=| Reader-stage | The work meets another mind | Meaning may exceed intention | Leave room for participation |
L001222|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0379|RAW=
L001223|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0380|RAW=### Core principle
L001224|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0381|RAW=
L001225|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0382|RAW=> **The piece becomes editable when it stops being identical to the self.**
L001226|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0383|RAW=
L001227|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0384|RAW=## 5.4 Brutal but sensitive
L001228|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0385|RAW=
L001229|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0386|RAW=This is the exact editorial posture needed.
L001230|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0387|RAW=
L001231|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0388|RAW=Brutal means:
L001232|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0389|RAW=
L001233|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0390|RAW=- remove what blocks entry;
L001234|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0391|RAW=- cut repeated explanation;
L001235|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0392|RAW=- delete impressive but unnecessary material;
L001236|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0393|RAW=- remove density that does not serve the piece;
L001237|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0394|RAW=- reduce self-protection language.
L001238|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0395|RAW=
L001239|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0396|RAW=Sensitive means:
L001240|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0397|RAW=
L001241|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0398|RAW=- protect the living charge;
L001242|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0399|RAW=- preserve the strange image if it carries truth;
L001243|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0400|RAW=- do not flatten mystery into generic clarity;
L001244|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0401|RAW=- keep rhythm, silence, and interior weather;
L001245|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0402|RAW=- respect the work’s own life.
L001246|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0403|RAW=
L001247|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0404|RAW=### Core principle
L001248|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0405|RAW=
L001249|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0406|RAW=> **Cut what blocks the life. Protect what carries it.**
L001250|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0407|RAW=
L001251|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0408|RAW=## 5.5 Theme plus metaphor as carrier system
L001252|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0409|RAW=
L001253|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0410|RAW=The reflections correctly identified theme and metaphor as heavy carriers.
L001254|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0411|RAW=
L001255|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0412|RAW=Theme carries continuity.
L001256|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0413|RAW=
L001257|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0414|RAW=Metaphor carries depth.
L001258|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0415|RAW=
L001259|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0416|RAW=Together they allow meaning to remain dense without forcing every meaning into explanation.
L001260|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0417|RAW=
L001261|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0418|RAW=### Carrier formula
L001262|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0419|RAW=
L001263|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0420|RAW=```text
L001264|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0421|RAW=Theme = the repeated field of concern.
L001265|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0422|RAW=Metaphor = the image-system that carries depth through the field.
L001266|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0423|RAW=Structure = the path the reader walks through the field.
L001267|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0424|RAW=Language = the local surface where meaning is spoken.
L001268|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0425|RAW=Silence = the space where the reader completes the field.
L001269|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0426|RAW=```
L001270|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0427|RAW=
L001271|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0428|RAW=---
L001272|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0429|RAW=
L001273|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0430|RAW=# 6. Meaning-carrier matrix
L001274|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0431|RAW=
L001275|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0432|RAW=Use this matrix when editing any dense piece.
L001276|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0433|RAW=
L001277|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0434|RAW=| Meaning type | Best carrier | Editing instruction |
L001278|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0435|RAW=|---|---|---|
L001279|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0436|RAW=| Literal argument | Direct language | Say it cleanly once |
L001280|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0437|RAW=| Emotional charge | Rhythm, image, scene | Do not over-explain the feeling |
L001281|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0438|RAW=| Mystery | Metaphor, silence, spacing | Protect ambiguity without making it obscure |
L001282|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0439|RAW=| Structure of thought | Headings, sequence, paragraph order | Let order do work that sentences are currently doing |
L001283|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0440|RAW=| Transformation | Before/after movement | Show the shift, do not only name it |
L001284|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0441|RAW=| Moral pressure | Conflict, image, restraint | Avoid preaching if the image can carry it |
L001285|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0442|RAW=| Source / unmanifested | Symbol, mythic frame, pattern | Give it a vessel, not a lecture |
L001286|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0443|RAW=| Professional credibility | Precision, restraint, evidence | Do not overclaim or inflate |
L001287|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0444|RAW=| Reader invitation | Opening clarity, concrete entry point | Give the reader a door |
L001288|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0445|RAW=| Subconscious pattern | Repetition, motif, recurring image | Let recurrence reveal what explanation cannot |
L001289|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0446|RAW=
L001290|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0447|RAW=---
L001291|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0448|RAW=
L001292|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0449|RAW=# 7. Source Voice translation
L001293|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0450|RAW=
L001294|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0451|RAW=## 7.1 The current pattern
L001295|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0452|RAW=
L001296|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0453|RAW=The current pattern can be stated as:
L001297|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0454|RAW=
L001298|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0455|RAW=```text
L001299|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0456|RAW=source first → structure second → reader third
L001300|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0457|RAW=```
L001301|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0458|RAW=
L001302|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0459|RAW=The event points toward a more complete sequence:
L001303|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0460|RAW=
L001304|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0461|RAW=```text
L001305|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0462|RAW=source → essence → vessel → reader
L001306|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0463|RAW=```
L001307|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0464|RAW=
L001308|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0465|RAW=## 7.2 What Source Voice is becoming
L001309|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0466|RAW=
L001310|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0467|RAW=Source Voice is not meant to become “more words.”
L001311|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0468|RAW=
L001312|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0469|RAW=It is meant to become clearer selection.
L001313|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0470|RAW=
L001314|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0471|RAW=The higher form of the voice is not the voice that says everything. It is the voice that knows:
L001315|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0472|RAW=
L001316|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0473|RAW=- what to reveal;
L001317|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0474|RAW=- what to imply;
L001318|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0475|RAW=- what to cut;
L001319|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0476|RAW=- what to let the image carry;
L001320|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0477|RAW=- what to let the reader discover;
L001321|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0478|RAW=- what to leave unsaid;
L001322|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0479|RAW=- what form the charge requires.
L001323|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0480|RAW=
L001324|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0481|RAW=## 7.3 Transition from channeling to authorship
L001325|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0482|RAW=
L001326|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0483|RAW=| Function | Role | Failure mode | Mature expression |
L001327|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0484|RAW=|---|---|---|---|
L001328|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0485|RAW=| Source | Brings the material | Overflow, totality pressure | Allows emergence |
L001329|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0486|RAW=| Author | Chooses the vessel | Self-protection, over-identification | Gives form and direction |
L001330|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0487|RAW=| Editor | Protects the reader and work | Flattening or over-cutting | Cuts congestion while preserving charge |
L001331|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0488|RAW=| Chair | Holds the guiding question | Drift and sprawl | Keeps the field coherent |
L001332|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0489|RAW=| Reader | Completes meaning | Misread risk | Receives and co-creates the final effect |
L001333|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0490|RAW=
L001334|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0491|RAW=### Core sentence
L001335|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0492|RAW=
L001336|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0493|RAW=> **Source gives the material. Author chooses the vessel. Editor protects the reader. Chair holds the question. Reader completes the field.**
L001337|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0494|RAW=
L001338|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0495|RAW=---
L001339|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0496|RAW=
L001340|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0497|RAW=# 8. Professional author lessons
L001341|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0498|RAW=
L001342|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0499|RAW=## 8.1 Main professional realization
L001343|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0500|RAW=
L001344|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0501|RAW=The event showed that published professional authors often do multiple things. They may earn, contribute, and develop through several overlapping language practices.
L001345|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0502|RAW=
L001346|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0503|RAW=This matters because it prevents the false belief that “being a writer” means one single output path.
L001347|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0504|RAW=
L001348|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0505|RAW=### Professional writing is often a portfolio
L001349|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0506|RAW=
L001350|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0507|RAW=Possible components include:
L001351|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0508|RAW=
L001352|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0509|RAW=| Professional component | What it can look like |
L001353|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0510|RAW=|---|---|
L001354|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0511|RAW=| Books | Fiction, poetry, essays, nonfiction, co-authored works |
L001355|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0512|RAW=| Editing | Editorial work, manuscript shaping, collaborative development |
L001356|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0513|RAW=| Teaching | Schools, universities, workshops, writing courses |
L001357|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0514|RAW=| Events | Readings, panels, author conversations, festivals |
L001358|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0515|RAW=| Commissions | Short pieces, public writing, poems for spaces, institutional writing |
L001359|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0516|RAW=| Fellowships / funds | Literary fund work, residencies, support roles, mentoring |
L001360|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0517|RAW=| Competitions | Recognition routes, prizes, publication opportunities |
L001361|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0518|RAW=| Publishing pathway | Agents, editors, publishers, small presses, literary journals |
L001362|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0519|RAW=| Collaboration | Co-authoring, shared-character fiction, relay writing, editorial partnerships |
L001363|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0520|RAW=| Reviewing / criticism | Writing about writing, books, culture, craft |
L001364|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0521|RAW=| Public artifacts | Poems on objects, local/community writing, small-format distribution |
L001365|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0522|RAW=| Advisory / coaching | Helping others with craft, structure, clarity, voice |
L001366|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0523|RAW=
L001367|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0524|RAW=## 8.2 Translation for the personal path
L001368|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0525|RAW=
L001369|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0526|RAW=Do not reduce the writing path to one book or one manuscript.
L001370|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0527|RAW=
L001371|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0528|RAW=The path may compound through:
L001372|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0529|RAW=
L001373|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0530|RAW=- manuscript work;
L001374|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0531|RAW=- essays;
L001375|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0532|RAW=- poems/fragments;
L001376|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0533|RAW=- Source Voice pieces;
L001377|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0534|RAW=- editorial diagnostics;
L001378|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0535|RAW=- offer clarity work;
L001379|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0536|RAW=- writing about writing;
L001380|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0537|RAW=- public readings or talks;
L001381|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0538|RAW=- workshops or teaching later;
L001382|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0539|RAW=- literary submissions;
L001383|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0540|RAW=- professional collaborations;
L001384|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0541|RAW=- editorial service offers;
L001385|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0542|RAW=- AI-assisted writing systems;
L001386|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0543|RAW=- decision-intelligence artifacts;
L001387|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0544|RAW=- public/private reflection files.
L001388|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0545|RAW=
L001389|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0546|RAW=### Core principle
L001390|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0547|RAW=
L001391|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0548|RAW=> **The work does not have to become one thing. It needs one clear next vessel at a time.**
L001392|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0549|RAW=
L001393|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0550|RAW=## 8.3 Professional author model: plurality without diffusion
L001394|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0551|RAW=
L001395|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0552|RAW=The risk of seeing multiple professional routes is over-expansion.
L001396|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0553|RAW=
L001397|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0554|RAW=The correction is:
L001398|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0555|RAW=
L001399|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0556|RAW=```text
L001400|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0557|RAW=Multiple future routes are allowed.
L001401|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0558|RAW=One current execution lane is selected.
L001402|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0559|RAW=```
L001403|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0560|RAW=
L001404|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0561|RAW=For now, the event should not create ten new projects. It should create one stronger editorial method and one clearer professional direction.
L001405|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0562|RAW=
L001406|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0563|RAW=---
L001407|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0564|RAW=
L001408|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0565|RAW=# 9. Editorial method from the event
L001409|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0566|RAW=
L001410|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0567|RAW=Use this as the primary method for dense work.
L001411|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0568|RAW=
L001412|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0569|RAW=| Pass | Name | Action | Question |
L001413|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0570|RAW=|---:|---|---|---|
L001414|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0571|RAW=| 1 | Source dump | Get the large material out | What is trying to come through? |
L001415|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0572|RAW=| 2 | Essence pass | Identify the central contribution | What is this piece actually giving? |
L001416|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0573|RAW=| 3 | Carrier map | Assign meaning to words, image, structure, metaphor, silence | Which carrier should hold which layer? |
L001417|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0574|RAW=| 4 | Theme pass | Find 2–3 repeated themes | What keeps returning? |
L001418|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0575|RAW=| 5 | Metaphor pass | Identify the heavy image-system | What image carries the depth? |
L001419|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0576|RAW=| 6 | Cut pass | Remove repetition, self-protection, congestion | What blocks entry? |
L001420|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0577|RAW=| 7 | Form pass | Choose vessel: essay, poem, prose-poem, mythic fragment, manifesto, hybrid | What form can hold the charge? |
L001421|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0578|RAW=| 8 | Reader pass | Test whether a stranger can enter | Can the reader feel the movement without needing the whole cosmology? |
L001422|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0579|RAW=| 9 | Brutal-sensitive edit | Cut hard, preserve life | What must go so the living thing can breathe? |
L001423|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0580|RAW=| 10 | Archive pass | Save before/after versions and lessons | What did this edit teach? |
L001424|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0581|RAW=
L001425|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0582|RAW=---
L001426|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0583|RAW=
L001427|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0584|RAW=# 10. Daily writer operating lessons
L001428|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0585|RAW=
L001429|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0586|RAW=## 10.1 Start with the main task
L001430|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0587|RAW=
L001431|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0588|RAW=One practical lesson from the event was that the day should open with the writing, not with news, email, external noise, or administrative scattering.
L001432|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0589|RAW=
L001433|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0590|RAW=### Rule
L001434|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0591|RAW=
L001435|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0592|RAW=> **Begin the day with the main writing or editorial task before external inputs.**
L001436|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0593|RAW=
L001437|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0594|RAW=## 10.2 Morning order
L001438|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0595|RAW=
L001439|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0596|RAW=Recommended order:
L001440|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0597|RAW=
L001441|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0598|RAW=1. Body/basic grounding.
L001442|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0599|RAW=2. Open the current piece.
L001443|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0600|RAW=3. Do one bounded writing or editing pass.
L001444|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0601|RAW=4. Save the receipt.
L001445|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0602|RAW=5. Only then check messages, news, email, admin, or feeds.
L001446|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0603|RAW=
L001447|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0604|RAW=## 10.3 Writing task types
L001448|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0605|RAW=
L001449|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0606|RAW=A day can count if it completes one of these:
L001450|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0607|RAW=
L001451|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0608|RAW=| Task | Minimum viable completion |
L001452|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0609|RAW=|---|---|
L001453|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0610|RAW=| Source writing | 300–1000 words raw |
L001454|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0611|RAW=| Essence pass | One paragraph naming the contribution |
L001455|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0612|RAW=| Cut pass | Remove one page, section, or cluster |
L001456|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0613|RAW=| Form pass | Decide vessel and restructure accordingly |
L001457|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0614|RAW=| Submission pass | Prepare one piece for external route |
L001458|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0615|RAW=| Reflection pass | Add one lesson to this master file |
L001459|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0616|RAW=| Professional pass | Map one professional route or income observation |
L001460|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0617|RAW=
L001461|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0618|RAW=## 10.4 Avoidance warning
L001462|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0619|RAW=
L001463|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0620|RAW=The danger is not only procrastination. It is also refinement as protective delay.
L001464|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0621|RAW=
L001465|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0622|RAW=The work can keep expanding internally to avoid closure.
L001466|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0623|RAW=
L001467|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0624|RAW=Corrective rule:
L001468|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0625|RAW=
L001469|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0626|RAW=> **Closure beats completeness when the purpose is learning through real contact.**
L001470|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0627|RAW=
L001471|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0628|RAW=---
L001472|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0629|RAW=
L001473|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0630|RAW=# 11. Reader relationship
L001474|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0631|RAW=
L001475|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0632|RAW=## 11.1 Writer and reader co-create meaning
L001476|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0633|RAW=
L001477|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0634|RAW=The writer makes their side.
L001478|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0635|RAW=
L001479|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0636|RAW=The reader receives, interprets, and completes.
L001480|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0637|RAW=
L001481|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0638|RAW=The work is therefore not controlled entirely by the writer.
L001482|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0639|RAW=
L001483|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0640|RAW=### Implication
L001484|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0641|RAW=
L001485|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0642|RAW=Trying to prevent all misinterpretation by adding more explanation can make the piece less readable.
L001486|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0643|RAW=
L001487|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0644|RAW=Better solution:
L001488|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0645|RAW=
L001489|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0646|RAW=- make the entry clear;
L001490|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0647|RAW=- make the movement coherent;
L001491|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0648|RAW=- let the image and structure carry depth;
L001492|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0649|RAW=- accept that some meaning will be completed by the reader.
L001493|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0650|RAW=
L001494|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0651|RAW=## 11.2 Reader-entry questions
L001495|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0652|RAW=
L001496|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0653|RAW=Before publishing or sharing, ask:
L001497|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0654|RAW=
L001498|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0655|RAW=| Question | Purpose |
L001499|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0656|RAW=|---|---|
L001500|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0657|RAW=| Where does the reader enter? | Prevents closed-circuit writing |
L001501|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0658|RAW=| What does the reader need in the first 10 seconds? | Improves immediate legibility |
L001502|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0659|RAW=| What can be felt instead of explained? | Reduces over-telling |
L001503|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0660|RAW=| What does the reader complete? | Creates participation |
L001504|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0661|RAW=| What must not be ambiguous? | Protects clarity |
L001505|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0662|RAW=| What can remain mysterious? | Protects depth |
L001506|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0663|RAW=
L001507|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0664|RAW=---
L001508|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0665|RAW=
L001509|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0666|RAW=# 12. Application to current manuscripts
L001510|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0667|RAW=
L001511|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0668|RAW=## 12.1 The 23-page source set
L001512|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0669|RAW=
L001513|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0670|RAW=Status:
L001514|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0671|RAW=
L001515|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0672|RAW=```text
L001516|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0673|RAW=The 23-page source set is the quarry, not the final stone.
L001517|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0674|RAW=```
L001518|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0675|RAW=
L001519|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0676|RAW=Do not judge it by whether every page belongs in the final manuscript. Judge it by whether it contains enough living material to extract from.
L001520|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0677|RAW=
L001521|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0678|RAW=## 12.2 The 1–3 page manuscript
L001522|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0679|RAW=
L001523|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0680|RAW=Status:
L001524|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0681|RAW=
L001525|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0682|RAW=```text
L001526|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0683|RAW=The 1–3 page manuscript is the cut stone.
L001527|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0684|RAW=```
L001528|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0685|RAW=
L001529|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0686|RAW=Its job is not to preserve every layer. Its job is to carry the living charge in a form another person can receive.
L001530|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0687|RAW=
L001531|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0688|RAW=## 12.3 Extraction method for the 23-page set
L001532|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0689|RAW=
L001533|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0690|RAW=Use this extraction table:
L001534|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0691|RAW=
L001535|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0692|RAW=| Step | Output |
L001536|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0693|RAW=|---|---|
L001537|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0694|RAW=| Identify the central contribution | One sentence |
L001538|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0695|RAW=| Mark the living images | 5–10 images or phrases |
L001539|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0696|RAW=| Mark repeated themes | 2–3 themes |
L001540|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0697|RAW=| Mark repeated explanations | Cut list |
L001541|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0698|RAW=| Choose form | Essay / prose poem / hybrid / fragment / manifesto |
L001542|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0699|RAW=| Draft compressed version | 1–3 pages |
L001543|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0700|RAW=| Read as stranger | Entry test |
L001544|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0701|RAW=| Cut again | 10–30% minimum unless already lean |
L001545|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0702|RAW=| Save cut log | Lessons preserved |
L001546|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0703|RAW=
L001547|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0704|RAW=## 12.4 Compression rule
L001548|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0705|RAW=
L001549|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0706|RAW=The compressed piece should not feel like a summary.
L001550|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0707|RAW=
L001551|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0708|RAW=It should feel like a concentrated form.
L001552|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0709|RAW=
L001553|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0710|RAW=Bad compression:
L001554|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0711|RAW=
L001555|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0712|RAW=> explains the larger work in fewer words.
L001556|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0713|RAW=
L001557|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0714|RAW=Good compression:
L001558|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0715|RAW=
L001559|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0716|RAW=> recreates the force of the larger work in a smaller vessel.
L001560|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0717|RAW=
L001561|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0718|RAW=---
L001562|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0719|RAW=
L001563|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0720|RAW=# 13. Lessons for public posts and Instagram/story writing
L001564|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0721|RAW=
L001565|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0722|RAW=## 13.1 Main problem
L001566|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0723|RAW=
L001567|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0724|RAW=Long dense reflections often do not land on Instagram because the platform rewards immediate entry, high visual readability, and clear emotional or practical hook.
L001568|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0725|RAW=
L001569|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0726|RAW=The issue is not that the thinking is weak. The issue is that the medium cannot carry the whole field at once.
L001570|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0727|RAW=
L001571|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0728|RAW=## 13.2 Platform translation
L001572|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0729|RAW=
L001573|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0730|RAW=| Source form | Instagram/story form |
L001574|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0731|RAW=|---|---|
L001575|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0732|RAW=| Full reflection | One distilled observation |
L001576|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0733|RAW=| Multi-layer concept | One image + one sentence |
L001577|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0734|RAW=| Long theory | Concrete example |
L001578|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0735|RAW=| Internal processing | Public-facing takeaway |
L001579|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0736|RAW=| Dense paragraph | 3–5 short lines |
L001580|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0737|RAW=| Universal claim | Personal observation with entry point |
L001581|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0738|RAW=
L001582|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0739|RAW=## 13.3 Story rule
L001583|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0740|RAW=
L001584|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0741|RAW=> **One story slide = one movement.**
L001585|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0742|RAW=
L001586|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0743|RAW=Do not ask one slide to carry:
L001587|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0744|RAW=
L001588|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0745|RAW=- background;
L001589|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0746|RAW=- theory;
L001590|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0747|RAW=- emotion;
L001591|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0748|RAW=- evidence;
L001592|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0749|RAW=- application;
L001593|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0750|RAW=- conclusion.
L001594|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0751|RAW=
L001595|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0752|RAW=Give each slide one job.
L001596|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0753|RAW=
L001597|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0754|RAW=---
L001598|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0755|RAW=
L001599|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0756|RAW=# 14. Universal sense-making model
L001600|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0757|RAW=
L001601|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0758|RAW=This model can be used across writing, business, outreach, art, and personal reflection.
L001602|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0759|RAW=
L001603|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0760|RAW=## 14.1 The universal sequence
L001604|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0761|RAW=
L001605|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0762|RAW=```text
L001606|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0763|RAW=Raw event
L001607|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0764|RAW=→ direct notes
L001608|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0765|RAW=→ pattern extraction
L001609|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0766|RAW=→ carrier assignment
L001610|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0767|RAW=→ practical method
L001611|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0768|RAW=→ future-use template
L001612|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0769|RAW=→ archive / master-file update
L001613|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0770|RAW=```
L001614|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0771|RAW=
L001615|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0772|RAW=## 14.2 The compounding question
L001616|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0773|RAW=
L001617|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0774|RAW=After any event, conversation, book, poem, film, client interaction, or manuscript session, ask:
L001618|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0775|RAW=
L001619|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0776|RAW=> **What did this teach that can become a reusable operating principle?**
L001620|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0777|RAW=
L001621|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0778|RAW=## 14.3 The sense-making table
L001622|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0779|RAW=
L001623|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0780|RAW=| Layer | Question | Output |
L001624|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0781|RAW=|---|---|---|
L001625|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0782|RAW=| Event | What happened? | Factual note |
L001626|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0783|RAW=| Signal | What stood out? | Highlight list |
L001627|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0784|RAW=| Pattern | What repeated? | Theme map |
L001628|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0785|RAW=| Principle | What is generally true here? | Reusable lesson |
L001629|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0786|RAW=| Method | How is it applied? | Checklist or sequence |
L001630|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0787|RAW=| Artifact | How is it preserved? | MD entry / prompt / template |
L001631|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0788|RAW=| Proof | Did it improve work? | Before/after example |
L001632|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0789|RAW=
L001633|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0790|RAW=---
L001634|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0791|RAW=
L001635|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0792|RAW=# 15. Professional path: writing as ecosystem
L001636|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0793|RAW=
L001637|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0794|RAW=## 15.1 Core observation
L001638|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0795|RAW=
L001639|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0796|RAW=Professional authors often survive and grow through a mixed ecology of work.
L001640|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0797|RAW=
L001641|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0798|RAW=This includes the published work, but also the surrounding functions:
L001642|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0799|RAW=
L001643|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0800|RAW=- teaching;
L001644|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0801|RAW=- speaking;
L001645|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0802|RAW=- editing;
L001646|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0803|RAW=- mentoring;
L001647|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0804|RAW=- reading;
L001648|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0805|RAW=- reviewing;
L001649|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0806|RAW=- collaborating;
L001650|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0807|RAW=- applying for opportunities;
L001651|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0808|RAW=- appearing in events;
L001652|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0809|RAW=- building relationships;
L001653|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0810|RAW=- learning craft;
L001654|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0811|RAW=- submitting work;
L001655|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0812|RAW=- accepting deadlines;
L001656|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0813|RAW=- making small pieces public.
L001657|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0814|RAW=
L001658|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0815|RAW=## 15.2 Personal application
L001659|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0816|RAW=
L001660|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0817|RAW=The current path can be held as a future ecosystem:
L001661|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0818|RAW=
L001662|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0819|RAW=| Lane | Possible expression | Current action |
L001663|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0820|RAW=|---|---|---|
L001664|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0821|RAW=| Manuscript lane | 1–3 page polished pieces, later book/collection | Build compressed manuscript outputs |
L001665|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0822|RAW=| Poetry / fragment lane | Source fragments, image-led pieces, small forms | Extract images and motifs |
L001666|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0823|RAW=| Editorial lane | Offer clarity, manuscript clarity, language diagnostics | Convert lessons into diagnostic method |
L001667|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0824|RAW=| Teaching / explanation lane | Writing about writing, sense-making guides | Keep this master file and produce usable frameworks |
L001668|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0825|RAW=| Event / speaking lane | Future readings, talks, workshops | Build clear pieces first |
L001669|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0826|RAW=| Collaboration lane | Co-writing, editorial partners, relay work | Practice making inner structure explicit |
L001670|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0827|RAW=| Professional submission lane | Competitions, journals, small presses | Prepare one clean piece at a time |
L001671|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0828|RAW=| Public artifact lane | Posts, PDFs, small downloadable pieces | Compress into platform-fit forms |
L001672|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0829|RAW=
L001673|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0830|RAW=## 15.3 Warning against premature expansion
L001674|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0831|RAW=
L001675|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0832|RAW=Do not open all lanes now.
L001676|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0833|RAW=
L001677|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0834|RAW=Use them as orientation, not immediate workload.
L001678|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0835|RAW=
L001679|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0836|RAW=Immediate focus:
L001680|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0837|RAW=
L001681|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0838|RAW=1. Build the editorial compression method.
L001682|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0839|RAW=2. Produce a small number of polished pieces.
L001683|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0840|RAW=3. Preserve lessons in this master file.
L001684|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0841|RAW=4. Test what lands with real readers.
L001685|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0842|RAW=5. Only then expand professional routes.
L001686|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0843|RAW=
L001687|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0844|RAW=---
L001688|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0845|RAW=
L001689|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0846|RAW=# 16. Reusable manuscript audit
L001690|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0847|RAW=
L001691|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0848|RAW=Use this whenever a piece feels overloaded.
L001692|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0849|RAW=
L001693|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0850|RAW=## 16.1 Audit questions
L001694|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0851|RAW=
L001695|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0852|RAW=| Question | Answer |
L001696|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0853|RAW=|---|---|
L001697|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0854|RAW=| What is the central contribution? |  |
L001698|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0855|RAW=| What is the main emotion underneath it? |  |
L001699|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0856|RAW=| What is the strongest image? |  |
L001700|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0857|RAW=| What is the governing metaphor? |  |
L001701|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0858|RAW=| What theme repeats? |  |
L001702|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0859|RAW=| What is over-explained? |  |
L001703|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0860|RAW=| What can structure carry instead of language? |  |
L001704|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0861|RAW=| What can image carry instead of explanation? |  |
L001705|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0862|RAW=| What can silence carry? |  |
L001706|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0863|RAW=| What must the reader know early? |  |
L001707|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0864|RAW=| What can the reader discover later? |  |
L001708|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0865|RAW=| What is the smallest vessel that still carries the charge? |  |
L001709|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0866|RAW=
