L001788|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0945|RAW=- Business writing:
L001789|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0946|RAW=- Public post:
L001790|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0947|RAW=- Personal reflection:
L001791|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0948|RAW=
L001792|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0949|RAW=### New operating principle
L001793|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0950|RAW=
L001794|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0951|RAW=> 
L001795|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0952|RAW=
L001796|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0953|RAW=### Receipt / proof of application
L001797|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0954|RAW=
L001798|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0955|RAW=- Piece edited:
L001799|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0956|RAW=- Before/after saved:

L001801|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0958|RAW=- Published / sent / archived:
L001802|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0959|RAW=```
L001803|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0960|RAW=

L001806|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0963|RAW=# 18. Version log

L001808|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0965|RAW=| Version | Date | Change |

L001813|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0970|RAW=
L001814|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0971|RAW=# 19. Open questions to carry forward
L001815|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0972|RAW=
L001816|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0973|RAW=These are not problems to solve immediately. They are active inquiry threads.
L001817|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0974|RAW=
L001818|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0975|RAW=1. What form is most natural for the Source Voice: essay, prose-poem, fragment, mythic nonfiction, diagnostic prose, or hybrid?
L001819|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0976|RAW=2. What kind of reader is most able to receive the work without requiring the full cosmology?
L001820|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0977|RAW=3. What is the first professional route worth testing: submission, public post, small PDF, reading, editorial service, or workshop?
L001821|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0978|RAW=4. How much explanation does the work actually need before image and structure can carry the rest?
L001822|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0979|RAW=5. Which current manuscript is closest to becoming “it” rather than “I”?
L001823|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0980|RAW=6. What recurring story keeps appearing in the writing, and what changes once it is noticed?
L001824|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0981|RAW=7. Which emotional fuel is present right now: anger, blame, grief, awe, pressure, longing, devotion, or discovery?
L001825|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0982|RAW=8. What is the smallest vessel that can carry the current charge?
L001826|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0983|RAW=
L001827|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0984|RAW=---
L001828|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0985|RAW=
L001829|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0986|RAW=# 20. Final distilled doctrine
L001830|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0987|RAW=
L001831|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0988|RAW=The event’s teaching can be carried as this doctrine:
L001832|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0989|RAW=
L001833|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0990|RAW=```text
L001834|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0991|RAW=Write the large field.
L001835|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0992|RAW=Find the central contribution.
L001836|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0993|RAW=Assign meaning to the right carriers.
L001837|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0994|RAW=Cut congestion without killing charge.
L001838|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0995|RAW=Let the work become it.
L001839|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0996|RAW=Let the reader complete the field.
L001840|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0997|RAW=Build writing as an ecosystem, not a single output.
L001841|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0998|RAW=Preserve every lesson as reusable method.
L001842|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=0999|RAW=```
L001843|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1000|RAW=
L001844|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1001|RAW=Or, in one line:
L001845|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1002|RAW=
L001846|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1003|RAW=> **Do not make the work smaller. Make the vessel truer.**
L001847|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1004|RAW=
L001848|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1005|RAW=
L001849|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1006|RAW=---
L001850|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1007|RAW=
L001851|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1008|RAW=# 21. Addendum v0.1.1 — Discipline, Ritual, Water, and Mode Entry
L001852|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1009|RAW=
L001853|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1010|RAW=## 21.1 Source reflection added
L001854|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1011|RAW=
L001855|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1012|RAW=A later reflection after the author event clarified another major lesson:
L001856|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1013|RAW=
L001857|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1014|RAW=> Writing can begin in abstraction, but it only becomes sustainable through rhythm, ritual, place, and repeated return.
L001858|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1015|RAW=
L001859|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1016|RAW=The event did not only teach editing and compression. It also showed that professional writing has a daily-life architecture around it. The work may be invisible, interior, symbolic, emotional, and abstract, but the author still needs practical anchors that let the body, attention, and mind enter the writing state again.
L001860|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1017|RAW=
L001861|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1018|RAW=This was especially clear in the references to:
L001862|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1019|RAW=
L001863|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1020|RAW=- discipline and routine;
L001864|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1021|RAW=- ritual objects;
L001865|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1022|RAW=- songs associated with a specific work;
L001866|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1023|RAW=- places that activate writing;
L001867|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1024|RAW=- water as a place of return and association;
L001868|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1025|RAW=- allowing the work to move in cycles rather than forcing it every day in the same way.
L001869|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1026|RAW=
L001870|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1027|RAW=## 21.2 Core addition
L001871|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1028|RAW=
L001872|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1029|RAW=The added lesson is:
L001873|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1030|RAW=
L001874|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1031|RAW=> **Abstraction needs a daily threshold.**
L001875|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1032|RAW=
L001876|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1033|RAW=A threshold is the repeatable condition that helps the writer cross from ordinary attention into creative attention.
L001877|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1034|RAW=
L001878|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1035|RAW=This can be:
L001879|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1036|RAW=
L001880|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1037|RAW=| Threshold type | Example | Function |
L001881|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1038|RAW=|---|---|---|
L001882|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1039|RAW=| Object | A notebook, pen, stone, cup, item on desk | Signals that the writing field is open |
L001883|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1040|RAW=| Song / sound | A track, playlist, ambient sound, silence | Creates emotional and nervous-system continuity |
L001884|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1041|RAW=| Place | Water, cafe, library, car, desk, walking route | Gives the work a physical container |
L001885|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1042|RAW=| Time | Morning, late night, pre-admin hour | Protects the writing before external noise enters |
L001886|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1043|RAW=| Gesture | Lighting something, opening a file, walking, making tea | Marks the transition into writing mode |
L001887|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1044|RAW=| Sequence | Body → place → object/song → piece → receipt | Turns inspiration into repeatable practice |
L001888|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1045|RAW=
L001889|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1046|RAW=The threshold is not superstition. It is a mode-entry technology.
L001890|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1047|RAW=
L001891|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1048|RAW=## 21.3 Ritual as mode-entry technology
L001892|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1049|RAW=
L001893|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1050|RAW=A ritual is useful when it lets the author return to the same inner field without needing to recreate the whole psychological condition from scratch.
L001894|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1051|RAW=
L001895|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1052|RAW=For dense Source Voice work, this matters because the writing does not always begin from a simple idea. It may begin from atmosphere, pressure, image, dream residue, inner charge, or a not-yet-verbal sense.
L001896|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1053|RAW=
L001897|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1054|RAW=The ritual gives the abstract field a handle.
L001898|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1055|RAW=
L001899|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1056|RAW=### Practical definition
L001900|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1057|RAW=
L001901|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1058|RAW=```text
L001902|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1059|RAW=Ritual = a repeatable external cue that helps the writer re-enter the internal field of a specific work.
L001903|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1060|RAW=```
L001904|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1061|RAW=
L001905|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1062|RAW=### What the ritual should do
L001906|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1063|RAW=
L001907|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1064|RAW=| Function | Meaning |
L001908|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1065|RAW=|---|---|
L001909|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1066|RAW=| Signal | “This is the piece I am entering.” |
L001910|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1067|RAW=| Contain | Prevent the whole life-field from flooding the page |
L001911|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1068|RAW=| Narrow | Select one manuscript, one mode, one vessel |
L001912|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1069|RAW=| Return | Make it easier to resume after time away |
L001913|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1070|RAW=| Protect | Hold the piece apart from news, admin, messages, and external noise |
L001914|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1071|RAW=| Embody | Bring the abstract work into body, place, sound, and rhythm |
L001915|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1072|RAW=
L001916|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1073|RAW=### What the ritual should not become
L001917|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1074|RAW=
L001918|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1075|RAW=| Failure mode | Warning |
L001919|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1076|RAW=|---|---|
L001920|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1077|RAW=| Dependency | “I cannot write unless the exact condition is present.” |
L001921|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1078|RAW=| Avoidance | Preparing the ritual replaces writing |
L001922|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1079|RAW=| Aesthetic theatre | The ritual looks meaningful but does not move the work |
L001923|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1080|RAW=| Over-complexity | Too many objects, songs, or steps create friction |
L001924|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1081|RAW=| Identity performance | The ritual becomes about being a writer rather than writing |
L001925|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1082|RAW=
L001926|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1083|RAW=### Operating principle
L001927|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1084|RAW=
L001928|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1085|RAW=> **The ritual exists to open the work, not to replace the work.**
L001929|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1086|RAW=
L001930|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1087|RAW=## 21.4 Object, song, and place as manuscript anchors
L001931|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1088|RAW=
L001932|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1089|RAW=The event suggested that a work may become associated with a particular item, song, or place. This is valuable because the work can become too abstract if it has no sensory anchor.
L001933|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1090|RAW=
L001934|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1091|RAW=### Anchor triad
L001935|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1092|RAW=
L001936|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1093|RAW=| Anchor | Best use | Question |
L001937|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1094|RAW=|---|---|---|
L001938|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1095|RAW=| Object | Stabilizing the work across sessions | What item reminds the body what piece this is? |
L001939|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1096|RAW=| Song / sound | Re-entering emotional atmosphere | What sound returns me to the correct inner weather? |
L001940|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1097|RAW=| Place | Holding the field physically | Where does this work naturally open? |
L001941|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1098|RAW=
L001942|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1099|RAW=### Application to current work
L001943|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1100|RAW=
L001944|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1101|RAW=For every serious piece, assign a small anchor set:
L001945|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1102|RAW=
L001946|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1103|RAW=```text
L001947|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1104|RAW=Piece title:
L001948|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1105|RAW=Object:
L001949|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1106|RAW=Song / sound:
L001950|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1107|RAW=Place:
L001951|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1108|RAW=Time window:
L001952|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1109|RAW=Opening gesture:
L001953|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1110|RAW=Closing receipt:
L001954|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1111|RAW=```
L001955|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1112|RAW=
L001956|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1113|RAW=This lets the manuscript become more than a file. It becomes a field with a repeatable doorway.
L001957|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1114|RAW=
L001958|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1115|RAW=## 21.5 Water as writing threshold
L001959|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1116|RAW=
L001960|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1117|RAW=Meg’s reference to water stood out because it connects directly with the Source Voice language of pre-field, source into form, unseen into seen, and unmanifested into manifest.
L001961|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1118|RAW=
L001962|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1119|RAW=Water can function as a symbolic and practical threshold.
L001963|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1120|RAW=
L001964|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1121|RAW=### Water symbolism in the work
L001965|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1122|RAW=
L001966|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1123|RAW=| Water function | Writing translation |
L001967|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1124|RAW=|---|---|
L001968|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1125|RAW=| Return | The work returns to source before taking form |
L001969|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1126|RAW=| Flow | Writing moves better when not over-forced |
L001970|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1127|RAW=| Reflection | The surface shows what is present without owning it |
L001971|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1128|RAW=| Depth | Meaning exists below what is immediately visible |
L001972|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1129|RAW=| Dissolution | Old form breaks down before new form appears |
L001973|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1130|RAW=| Emergence | The unseen becomes visible through movement |
L001974|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1131|RAW=| Cleansing | Noise and residue are washed off before entering the piece |
L001975|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1132|RAW=
L001976|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1133|RAW=### Practical water rituals
L001977|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1134|RAW=
L001978|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1135|RAW=| Ritual | Use |
L001979|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1136|RAW=|---|---|
L001980|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1137|RAW=| Walk near water before drafting | Open source field without forcing language |
L001981|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1138|RAW=| Sit by water after a draft | Let the piece settle before cutting |
L001982|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1139|RAW=| Use water sounds while editing | Maintain flow while applying form-pressure |
L001983|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1140|RAW=| Wash hands before writing | Mark transition from ordinary mode to writing mode |
L001984|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1141|RAW=| Carry water/tea into session | Give the body a simple continuity object |
L001985|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1142|RAW=| Use water imagery intentionally | Let the symbol carry pre-field/source/form movement |
L001986|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1143|RAW=
L001987|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1144|RAW=### Core principle
L001988|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1145|RAW=
L001989|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1146|RAW=> **Water is not only scenery. It can be a return-point between the unformed and the formed.**
L001990|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1147|RAW=
L001991|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1148|RAW=## 21.6 Flow, off-days, and cyclical writing
L001992|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1149|RAW=
L001993|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1150|RAW=Another important realization is that the current stage is no longer primarily about struggling to find what to write about.
L001994|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1151|RAW=
L001995|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1152|RAW=There will still be days when writing turns on and days when it turns off. That does not mean the path is lost. It means writing has cycles.
L001996|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1153|RAW=
L001997|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1154|RAW=The mature move is to go with the flow without abandoning discipline.
L001998|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1155|RAW=
L001999|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1156|RAW=### Distinction
L002000|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1157|RAW=
L002001|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1158|RAW=| State | Meaning | Correct action |
L002002|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1159|RAW=|---|---|---|
L002003|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1160|RAW=| Writing-on day | The field is open; language is available | Draft, extend, capture, let material come |
L002004|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1161|RAW=| Writing-off day | Language is closed but the path remains | Edit, read, walk, organize, submit, reflect, rest |
L002005|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1162|RAW=| Pressure day | Energy is present but unstable | Use form-pressure: small poem, fragment, 20-minute cut |
L002006|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1163|RAW=| Integration day | Previous material needs settling | Re-read, tag themes, update master file |
L002007|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1164|RAW=| Professional day | The writing ecosystem needs action | Submit, research route, email, format, archive |
L002008|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1165|RAW=| Recovery day | Body/attention cannot carry deep work | Protect continuity with one small receipt |
L002009|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1166|RAW=
L002010|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1167|RAW=### Key correction
L002011|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1168|RAW=
L002012|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1169|RAW=Do not confuse an off-day with the absence of vocation.
L002013|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1170|RAW=
L002014|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1171|RAW=An off-day may still serve the writing if it keeps the ecosystem alive.
L002015|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1172|RAW=
L002016|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1173|RAW=### Minimum receipt on off-days
L002017|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1174|RAW=
L002018|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1175|RAW=When writing is closed, complete one of these:
L002019|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1176|RAW=
L002020|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1177|RAW=- read one page of the current work;
L002021|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1178|RAW=- mark one phrase that still has life;
L002022|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1179|RAW=- cut one unnecessary paragraph;
L002023|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1180|RAW=- add one note to this master file;
L002024|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1181|RAW=- identify tomorrow’s first writing action;
L002025|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1182|RAW=- walk with the piece in mind;
L002026|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1183|RAW=- return to the anchor object/song/place for five minutes.
L002027|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1184|RAW=
L002028|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1185|RAW=### Operating principle
L002029|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1186|RAW=
L002030|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1187|RAW=> **Flow is allowed. Drift is not.**
L002031|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1188|RAW=
L002032|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1189|RAW=## 21.7 Updated daily writing rhythm
L002033|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1190|RAW=
L002034|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1191|RAW=The previous daily writer operating lesson stays intact: begin with the main writing or editorial task before external inputs.
L002035|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1192|RAW=
L002036|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1193|RAW=This addendum adds a ritualized entry sequence.
L002037|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1194|RAW=
L002038|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1195|RAW=### Standard writing-day sequence
L002039|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1196|RAW=
L002040|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1197|RAW=| Step | Action | Purpose |
L002041|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1198|RAW=|---:|---|---|
L002042|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1199|RAW=| 1 | Basic body grounding | Make the body available |
L002043|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1200|RAW=| 2 | Select the piece | Prevent abstract sprawl |
L002044|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1201|RAW=| 3 | Activate the anchor | Object, song, place, water, or gesture |
L002045|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1202|RAW=| 4 | Name the session type | Draft / cut / structure / image / submission / reflection |
L002046|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1203|RAW=| 5 | Work for a bounded window | Avoid endless field expansion |
L002047|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1204|RAW=| 6 | Save a receipt | Preserve proof of continuity |
L002048|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1205|RAW=| 7 | Close the field deliberately | Prevent the piece from leaking into the whole day |
L002049|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1206|RAW=
L002050|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1207|RAW=### Session-type menu
L002051|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1208|RAW=
L002052|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1209|RAW=| Session type | Output |
L002053|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1210|RAW=|---|---|
L002054|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1211|RAW=| Source session | Raw material captured |
L002055|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1212|RAW=| Essence session | One central contribution named |
L002056|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1213|RAW=| Water session | Walk/sit/reflect until the next image appears |
L002057|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1214|RAW=| Form session | Vessel selected or adjusted |
L002058|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1215|RAW=| Cut session | Congestion removed |
L002059|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1216|RAW=| Image session | Strongest image identified or refined |
L002060|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1217|RAW=| Ritual session | Anchor set tested |
L002061|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1218|RAW=| Submission session | Work moved toward professional route |
L002062|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1219|RAW=| Archive session | Lesson stored in this file |
L002063|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1220|RAW=
L002064|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1221|RAW=### One-line rule
L002065|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1222|RAW=
L002066|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1223|RAW=> **Enter through ritual. Work through discipline. Exit with receipt.**
L002067|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1224|RAW=

L002117|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1274|RAW=## 21.9 Application to Source Voice and pre-field work
L002118|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1275|RAW=
L002119|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1276|RAW=This lesson integrates strongly with the pre-field/source/form language.
L002120|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1277|RAW=
L002121|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1278|RAW=The writing process can now be framed as:
L002122|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1279|RAW=
L002123|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1280|RAW=```text
L002124|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1281|RAW=Pre-field / unmanifested
L002125|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1282|RAW=→ sensed through body, place, rhythm, water, image
L002126|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1283|RAW=→ entered through ritual
L002127|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1284|RAW=→ captured through source draft
L002128|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1285|RAW=→ shaped through vessel
L002129|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1286|RAW=→ cut through editorial discipline
L002130|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1287|RAW=→ received by reader
L002131|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1288|RAW=→ returned to archive as lesson
L002132|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1289|RAW=```
L002133|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1290|RAW=
L002134|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1291|RAW=This makes ritual part of the bridge between invisible and visible.
L002135|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1292|RAW=
L002136|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1293|RAW=It also prevents the work from staying only in abstract consciousness.
L002137|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1294|RAW=
L002138|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1295|RAW=### Key implication
L002139|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1296|RAW=
L002140|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1297|RAW=> **The unseen does not become seen through thought alone. It becomes seen through repeated embodied return.**
L002141|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1298|RAW=
L002142|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1299|RAW=## 21.10 Updated doctrine
L002143|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1300|RAW=
L002144|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1301|RAW=The author-event doctrine now expands from editorial compression into daily creative embodiment.
L002145|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1302|RAW=
L002146|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1303|RAW=```text
L002147|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1304|RAW=Write the large field.
L002148|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1305|RAW=Find the central contribution.
L002149|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1306|RAW=Assign meaning to the right carriers.
L002150|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1307|RAW=Choose a vessel.
L002151|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1308|RAW=Create a threshold into the work.
L002152|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1309|RAW=Use ritual to enter.
L002153|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1310|RAW=Use discipline to continue.
L002154|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1311|RAW=Use water, object, song, or place to return.
L002155|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1312|RAW=Cut congestion without killing charge.
L002156|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1313|RAW=Let the work become it.
L002157|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1314|RAW=Let the reader complete the field.
L002158|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1315|RAW=Respect off-days without drifting.
L002159|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1316|RAW=Build writing as an ecosystem, not a single output.
L002160|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1317|RAW=Preserve every lesson as reusable method.
L002161|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1318|RAW=```
L002162|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1319|RAW=
L002163|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1320|RAW=One-line expansion:
L002164|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1321|RAW=
L002165|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1322|RAW=> **Do not only ask what the work means. Ask what daily threshold lets the work return.**
L002166|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1323|RAW=
L002167|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1324|RAW=## 21.11 Future inquiry threads from this addendum
L002168|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1325|RAW=
L002169|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1326|RAW=1. Which current manuscript already has a natural place, song, object, or water association?
L002170|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1327|RAW=2. What is the first piece that should receive a full manuscript ritual map?
L002171|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1328|RAW=3. Does water function as symbol, place, rhythm, or all three in the current body of work?
L002172|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1329|RAW=4. What is the minimum off-day receipt that preserves continuity without forcing output?
L002173|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1330|RAW=5. Which ritual makes the work easier to enter, and which ritual becomes avoidance?
L002174|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1331|RAW=6. How can daily rhythm support Source Voice without turning it into mechanical productivity?
L002175|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1332|RAW=7. What is the difference between flow and drift in the current writing practice?
L002176|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1333|RAW=8. How can professional discipline coexist with receptivity to the unmanifested?

Existing sections retained unchanged; this is an additive expansion. |

L002187|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1344|RAW=
L002188|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1345|RAW=# 23. Addendum v0.1.2 — Editorial Recognition as the Missing Function
L002189|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1346|RAW=
L002190|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1347|RAW=## 23.1 Source reflection added
L002191|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1348|RAW=
L002192|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1349|RAW=A later reflection clarified the central personal/craft realization produced by the event:
L002193|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1350|RAW=
L002194|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1351|RAW=> **The missing function was editorial.**
L002195|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1352|RAW=
L002196|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1353|RAW=Before attending the author event, the issue was already being sensed through language, density, reader-legibility problems, manuscript length, source overload, and the repeated question of how to make the work land. The need was present, but it had not yet been named as an editorial need.
L002197|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1354|RAW=
L002198|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1355|RAW=The event supplied the anchoring point. It made visible that the problem was not a lack of source, not a lack of meaning, not a lack of depth, and not even primarily a lack of writing. The missing layer was the professional act of shaping: choosing the vessel, cutting congestion, assigning meaning to the right carriers, and protecting the reader from overload without betraying the source.
L002199|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1356|RAW=
L002200|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1357|RAW=This realization should now be preserved as an additive layer to the existing author-event file and all related manuscript-development files.
L002201|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1358|RAW=
L002202|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1359|RAW=## 23.2 What was sensed before the event
L002203|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1360|RAW=
L002204|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1361|RAW=The pre-event state can be described as a correct but unnamed perception.
L002205|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1362|RAW=
L002206|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1363|RAW=The live questions were already orbiting the editorial layer:
L002207|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1364|RAW=
L002208|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1365|RAW=- Why does the material feel powerful but not always land?
L002209|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1366|RAW=- Why does the large manuscript carry the truth but still feel too much for the reader?
L002210|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1367|RAW=- How can the source remain intact without the output becoming dump-like?
L002211|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1368|RAW=- How much should be language, how much structure, and how much image?
L002212|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1369|RAW=- What should be cut without losing the living charge?
L002213|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1370|RAW=- What should stay implicit instead of being explained?
L002214|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1371|RAW=- How does a manuscript become readable without becoming smaller in soul?
L002215|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1372|RAW=
L002216|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1373|RAW=At that stage, the perception existed through pressure rather than name.
L002217|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1374|RAW=
L002218|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1375|RAW=The work was already calling for editing, but the word **editing** had not yet become the stable container.
L002219|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1376|RAW=
L002220|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1377|RAW=## 23.3 What the event anchored
L002221|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1378|RAW=
L002222|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1379|RAW=The event converted a felt problem into a named function.
L002223|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1380|RAW=
L002224|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1381|RAW=The author conversation showed that professional writing is not only expression. It is also:
L002225|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1382|RAW=
L002226|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1383|RAW=| Function | Meaning |
L002227|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1384|RAW=|---|---|
L002228|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1385|RAW=| Selection | Choosing what belongs in the vessel now. |
L002229|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1386|RAW=| Compression | Reducing overload so the charge can travel. |
L002230|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1387|RAW=| Form-pressure | Letting constraint make meaning available. |
L002231|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1388|RAW=| Reader protection | Preventing the reader from being flooded by the whole source field. |
L002232|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1389|RAW=| Carrier assignment | Deciding what is carried by language, image, metaphor, structure, silence, rhythm, or reader participation. |
L002233|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1390|RAW=| Externalization | Making inner architecture shareable enough for another mind to enter. |
L002234|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1391|RAW=| Objectification | Letting the work become “it” rather than remaining fused with “I.” |
L002235|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1392|RAW=
L002236|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1393|RAW=The event therefore did not merely provide advice. It provided recognition.
L002237|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1394|RAW=
L002238|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1395|RAW=> **The work did not need less source. It needed editorial mediation.**
L002239|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1396|RAW=
L002240|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1397|RAW=## 23.4 Editorial as the missing bridge
L002241|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1398|RAW=
L002242|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1399|RAW=The editorial layer sits between source and reader.
L002243|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1400|RAW=
L002244|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1401|RAW=```text
L002245|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1402|RAW=SOURCE
L002246|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1403|RAW=→ raw field, charge, image, memory, metaphysics, rupture, pattern
L002247|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1404|RAW=
L002248|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1405|RAW=AUTHOR
L002249|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1406|RAW=→ chooses the vessel and central contribution
L002250|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1407|RAW=
L002251|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1408|RAW=EDITORIAL
L002252|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1409|RAW=→ cuts congestion, orders carriers, protects reader access
L002253|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1410|RAW=
L002254|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1411|RAW=READER
L002255|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1412|RAW=→ receives, interprets, completes the field
L002256|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1413|RAW=```
L002257|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1414|RAW=
L002258|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1415|RAW=Before this realization, source and reader were sometimes too close together. The work tried to carry the full field directly into reception. That produced power, but also congestion.
L002259|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1416|RAW=
L002260|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1417|RAW=The editorial layer creates a humane distance.
L002261|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1418|RAW=
L002262|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1419|RAW=It does not betray the source. It lets the source survive contact with another mind.
L002263|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1420|RAW=
L002264|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1421|RAW=## 23.5 Key correction to the writing process
L002265|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1422|RAW=
L002266|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1423|RAW=The correction is simple but decisive:
L002267|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1424|RAW=
L002268|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1425|RAW=> **Do not solve every manuscript problem by writing more. Some manuscript problems are solved by editing.**
L002269|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1426|RAW=
L002270|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1427|RAW=This applies especially when the source is already strong.
L002271|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1428|RAW=
L002272|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1429|RAW=| Old impulse | Editorial correction |
L002273|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1430|RAW=|---|---|
L002274|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1431|RAW=| Add more explanation. | Cut repeated explanation and let image/structure carry. |
L002275|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1432|RAW=| Preserve every layer in the main text. | Move some layers into archive, appendix, or silence. |
L002276|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1433|RAW=| Make the reader understand the whole system. | Give the reader a clear door and one living movement. |
L002277|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1434|RAW=| Treat cutting as loss. | Treat cutting as transmission. |
L002278|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1435|RAW=| Defend the source through density. | Protect the source through proportion. |
L002279|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1436|RAW=| Keep the work fused with self. | Let the work become an object that can be shaped. |
L002280|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1437|RAW=
L002281|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1438|RAW=## 23.6 The new core editorial sentence
L002282|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1439|RAW=
L002283|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1440|RAW=The event-reflection doctrine can now be sharpened:
L002284|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1441|RAW=
L002285|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1442|RAW=> **Source gives the material. Author chooses the vessel. Editorial makes the vessel receivable. Reader completes the field.**
L002286|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1443|RAW=
L002287|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1444|RAW=This is a refinement of the earlier line:
L002288|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1445|RAW=
L002289|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1446|RAW=> Source gives the material. Author chooses the vessel. Editor protects the reader.
L002290|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1447|RAW=
L002291|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1448|RAW=Both remain valid. The newer phrasing makes clear that editorial is not only an external person. It is also an internal function that can be learned, practiced, and applied.
L002292|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1449|RAW=
L002293|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1450|RAW=## 23.7 Editorial recognition and the two manuscripts
L002294|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1451|RAW=
L002295|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1452|RAW=This realization also clarifies the relationship between the current manuscripts.
L002296|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1453|RAW=
L002297|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1454|RAW=| Manuscript | Source function | Editorial need now visible |
L002298|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1455|RAW=|---|---|---|
L002299|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1456|RAW=| **The Pre-Form Architecture** | Carries the metaphysical/civilizational field: source, form, Giza, capstone, language, technology, governance, responsibility. | Needs vessel-selection so the reader receives the architecture without being overwhelmed by the whole lattice. |
L002300|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1457|RAW=| **The Measure of Return** | Carries the moral/personal field: rupture, proportion, accountability, substrate, sovereignty, repair. | Needs proportion-control so testimony remains authored, accountable, and readable without becoming defense or over-explanation. |
L002301|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1458|RAW=| **1–3 page pieces** | Carry the distilled public-facing charge. | Need compression without becoming summary. |
L002302|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1459|RAW=| **23-page source set** | Acts as quarry/source reservoir. | Needs extraction, not full preservation in every smaller vessel. |
L002303|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1460|RAW=| **369-page lattice** | Acts as archive/expansion field. | Needs protection from becoming the reader-facing default. |
L002304|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1461|RAW=
L002305|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1462|RAW=## 23.8 Editorial as a Source Voice function
L002306|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1463|RAW=
L002307|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1464|RAW=Source Voice is not only the ability to receive or articulate source material.
L002308|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1465|RAW=
L002309|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1466|RAW=Source Voice matures when it can also edit.
L002310|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1467|RAW=
L002311|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1468|RAW=The higher form of Source Voice is not more total speech. It is accurate selection.
L002312|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1469|RAW=
L002313|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1470|RAW=It knows:
L002314|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1471|RAW=
L002315|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1472|RAW=- what must be said;
L002316|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1473|RAW=- what must be structured;
L002317|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1474|RAW=- what must be imaged;
L002318|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1475|RAW=- what must be left silent;
L002319|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1476|RAW=- what must be cut;
L002320|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1477|RAW=- what belongs in a source file but not a public piece;
L002321|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1478|RAW=- what belongs in the body and what belongs in an appendix;
L002322|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1479|RAW=- what the reader can receive now;
L002323|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1480|RAW=- what the work can safely become in this vessel.
L002324|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1481|RAW=
L002325|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1482|RAW=### Core principle
L002326|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1483|RAW=
L002327|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1484|RAW=> **The source may be infinite, but the vessel must be finite. Editorial is the art of choosing the finite form without betraying the infinite charge.**
L002328|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1485|RAW=
L002329|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1486|RAW=## 23.9 Updated operating sequence
L002330|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1487|RAW=
L002331|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1488|RAW=The writing process should now include editorial recognition as an explicit phase.
L002332|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1489|RAW=
L002333|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1490|RAW=```text
L002334|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1491|RAW=1. Source arises.
L002335|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1492|RAW=2. Source is captured without premature judgment.
L002336|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1493|RAW=3. The central contribution is named.
L002337|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1494|RAW=4. The vessel is selected.
L002338|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1495|RAW=5. Meaning is assigned across carriers.
L002339|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1496|RAW=6. Editorial cuts congestion.
L002340|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1497|RAW=7. The work becomes “it.”
L002341|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1498|RAW=8. Reader-entry is tested.
L002342|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1499|RAW=9. Final form is produced.
L002343|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1500|RAW=10. Lessons are archived.
L002344|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1501|RAW=```
L002345|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1502|RAW=
L002346|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1503|RAW=### Practical editing question
L002347|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1504|RAW=
L002348|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1505|RAW=Before any new output is expanded, ask:
L002349|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1506|RAW=
L002350|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1507|RAW=> **Is this a writing problem, or is it now an editing problem?**
L002351|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1508|RAW=
L002352|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1509|RAW=If the source is missing, write.
L002353|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1510|RAW=
L002354|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1511|RAW=If the source is present but overloaded, edit.
L002355|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1512|RAW=
L002356|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1513|RAW=If the piece is powerful but not landing, edit.
L002357|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1514|RAW=
L002358|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1515|RAW=If the reader cannot enter, edit.
L002359|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1516|RAW=
L002360|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1517|RAW=If the author is defending the whole field through density, edit.
L002361|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1518|RAW=
L002362|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1519|RAW=## 23.10 Additive use with existing MD files
L002363|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1520|RAW=
L002364|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1521|RAW=This addendum should not replace the existing author-event MD material.
L002365|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1522|RAW=
L002366|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1523|RAW=It should be appended to it and treated as a later recognition layer.
L002367|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1524|RAW=
L002368|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1525|RAW=The earlier sections preserve the event map, author functions, compression doctrine, writing ecosystem, and ritual/water threshold. This addendum adds the missing meta-recognition:
L002369|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1526|RAW=
L002370|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1527|RAW=> **The event revealed that the unnamed need was editorial.**
L002371|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1528|RAW=
L002372|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1529|RAW=This should also inform future manuscript files, especially:
L002373|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1530|RAW=
L002374|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1531|RAW=- Pre-Form Architecture source/manuscript files;
L002375|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1532|RAW=- Measure of Return manuscript files;
L002376|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1533|RAW=- 1–3 page public-facing compression pieces;
L002377|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1534|RAW=- Source Voice operating files;
L002378|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1535|RAW=- future event reflection files;
L002379|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1536|RAW=- manuscript audit templates.
L002380|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1537|RAW=
L002381|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1538|RAW=## 23.11 Immediate application rules
L002382|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1539|RAW=
L002383|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1540|RAW=For the next manuscript pass, apply the following:
L002384|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1541|RAW=
L002385|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1542|RAW=| Rule | Application |
L002386|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1543|RAW=|---|---|
L002387|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1544|RAW=| Keep source files expansive. | Let source fields remain complete in archive/manuscript form. |
L002388|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1545|RAW=| Make public vessels finite. | Do not carry the whole lattice into every output. |
L002389|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1546|RAW=| Cut congestion, not charge. | Preserve the living image, remove repeated explanation. |
L002390|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1547|RAW=| Assign carriers. | Let structure, metaphor, rhythm, and silence do work that prose is over-carrying. |
L002391|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1548|RAW=| Test reader entry. | The reader should know where they are within the first few lines. |
L002392|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1549|RAW=| Preserve before/after. | Save each compression as proof of editorial learning. |
L002393|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1550|RAW=| Let the piece become “it.” | Edit the work as object, not as self-defense. |
L002394|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1551|RAW=
L002395|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1552|RAW=## 23.12 One-line doctrine update
L002396|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1553|RAW=
L002397|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1554|RAW=The updated doctrine is:
L002398|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1555|RAW=
L002399|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1556|RAW=> **Write until the source appears. Edit until the vessel can carry it.**
L002400|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1557|RAW=
L002401|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1558|RAW=Or, more fully:
L002402|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1559|RAW=
L002403|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1560|RAW=```text
L002404|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1561|RAW=The source was not missing.
L002405|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1562|RAW=The editorial layer was missing.
L002406|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1563|RAW=The event named it.
L002407|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1564|RAW=Now the work can move from expression into authorship.
L002408|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1565|RAW=```
L002409|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1566|RAW=
L002410|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1567|RAW=## 23.13 Future inquiry threads
L002411|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1568|RAW=
L002412|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1569|RAW=1. Which current pieces are still being treated as writing problems when they are actually editing problems?
L002413|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1570|RAW=2. What is the smallest vessel that can carry each manuscript’s charge?
L002414|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1571|RAW=3. What parts of the current work should be carried by image rather than explanation?
L002415|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1572|RAW=4. What parts should be carried by structure rather than prose?
L002416|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1573|RAW=5. What parts belong in archive, not reader-facing form?
L002417|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1574|RAW=6. Where is density still being used as protection?
L002418|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1575|RAW=7. Which piece is ready to become “it”?
L002419|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1576|RAW=8. What would an external editor protect the reader from in the current work?
L002420|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1577|RAW=9. What would an external editor fight to preserve because it carries the life?
L002421|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1578|RAW=10. What is the next before/after edit that proves this lesson has become practice?
L002422|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1579|RAW=
