L002432|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1589|RAW=
L002433|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1590|RAW=# 25. Addendum v0.1.3 — Writing, Self-Rediscovery, and Work-Phase Transformation
L002434|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1591|RAW=
L002435|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1592|RAW=## 25.1 Source reflection added
L002436|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1593|RAW=
L002437|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1594|RAW=A further question arose after the event and after the editorial-recognition layer was added:
L002438|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1595|RAW=
L002439|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1596|RAW=> If writing creates self-rediscovery, where does that process end? Does redefining and rediscovery continue forever, or does the writer eventually become a greater master of direction?
L002440|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1597|RAW=
L002441|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1598|RAW=This question belongs inside the author-event file because it clarifies what happens after the source has appeared and after the editorial function has been recognized.
L002442|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1599|RAW=
L002443|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1600|RAW=The answer is phase-based.
L002444|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1601|RAW=
L002445|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1602|RAW=Writing does not stop revealing the self. But the role of that revelation changes.
L002446|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1603|RAW=
L002447|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1604|RAW=At first, the work may function as mirror, witness, repair chamber, source-field, and self-recovery instrument. The writing is still close to “I.” Cutting it can feel like cutting the self, because the piece is still carrying identity-continuity, pain, explanation, moral repair, and authorship-recovery.
L002448|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1605|RAW=
L002449|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1606|RAW=Later, the work becomes “it.” It has its own shape, pressure, rhythm, contribution, limits, and reader-path. At this point the author can edit it without treating every cut as self-erasure.
L002450|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1607|RAW=
L002451|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1608|RAW=The work has changed face.
L002452|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1609|RAW=
L002453|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1610|RAW=It is no longer the same type of work throughout the entire process.
L002454|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1611|RAW=
L002455|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1612|RAW=## 25.2 Core recognition
L002456|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1613|RAW=
L002457|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1614|RAW=The major recognition is not only that editing was missing.
L002458|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1615|RAW=
L002459|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1616|RAW=It is that the work changes function as it develops.
L002460|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1617|RAW=
L002461|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1618|RAW=A piece may begin as self-discovery, become self-repair, then become manuscript, then become object, then become public vessel, then become reader-field, then become archived lesson.
L002462|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1619|RAW=
L002463|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1620|RAW=If those phases are collapsed into one, the author may keep asking the wrong question.
L002464|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1621|RAW=
L002465|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1622|RAW=| Phase | Wrong question if phase is misread | Better question |
L002466|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1623|RAW=|---|---|---|
L002467|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1624|RAW=| Source emergence | “Is this publishable yet?” | What is trying to come through? |
L002468|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1625|RAW=| Self-discovery | “Why is this still so personal?” | What part of the self is being recognized? |
L002469|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1626|RAW=| Identity-repair | “Why can’t I cut this?” | What is this piece still carrying for the self? |
L002470|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1627|RAW=| It-stage | “Does this still represent all of me?” | What does the work need as an object? |
L002471|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1628|RAW=| Editorial stage | “Am I betraying the source by cutting?” | What must be removed so the source can travel? |
L002472|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1629|RAW=| Reader stage | “How do I control every interpretation?” | What does the reader need to enter and complete the field? |
L002473|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1630|RAW=| Archive stage | “Was this final?” | What did this version teach for the next vessel? |
L002474|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1631|RAW=
L002475|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1632|RAW=## 25.3 Core distinction
L002476|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1633|RAW=
L002477|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1634|RAW=There are two kinds of rediscovery:
L002478|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1635|RAW=
L002479|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1636|RAW=| Type | Function | Endpoint |
L002480|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1637|RAW=|---|---|---|
L002481|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1638|RAW=| Identity-repair rediscovery | Writing restores continuity after rupture, pressure, silence, misread, or fragmentation. | This should stabilize. |
L002482|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1639|RAW=| Living-art rediscovery | Writing continues to reveal new relation between self, world, language, reader, mystery, image, and form. | This continues indefinitely. |
L002483|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1640|RAW=
L002484|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1641|RAW=The goal is not to end discovery.
L002485|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1642|RAW=
L002486|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1643|RAW=The goal is to end the need for every work to rescue the self.
L002487|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1644|RAW=
L002488|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1645|RAW=## 25.4 Phase movement
L002489|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1646|RAW=
L002490|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1647|RAW=```text
L002491|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1648|RAW=I-stage
L002492|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1649|RAW=→ It-stage
L002493|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1650|RAW=→ Craft-stage
L002494|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1651|RAW=→ Transmission-stage
L002495|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1652|RAW=→ Mastery-stage
L002496|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1653|RAW=```
L002497|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1654|RAW=
L002498|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1655|RAW=| Phase | Description | Primary function |
L002499|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1656|RAW=|---|---|---|
L002500|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1657|RAW=| I-stage | The work feels identical to the self. Writing discovers and repairs identity. | Recognition |
L002501|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1658|RAW=| It-stage | The work becomes an object. It can be edited, shaped, and tested. | Separation |
L002502|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1659|RAW=| Craft-stage | The author chooses vessels rather than flooding every vessel with the whole field. | Formation |
L002503|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1660|RAW=| Transmission-stage | The work meets readers and becomes completed partly through reception. | Exchange |
L002504|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1661|RAW=| Mastery-stage | Rediscovery continues, but through direction, craft, service, and repeatable form. | Stewardship |
L002505|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1662|RAW=
L002506|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1663|RAW=## 25.5 Why the work changes face
L002507|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1664|RAW=
L002508|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1665|RAW=A manuscript does not remain one thing from beginning to end.
L002509|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1666|RAW=
L002510|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1667|RAW=It may look like the same file, the same title, or the same body of text, but its function changes as the author’s relation to it changes.
L002511|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1668|RAW=
L002512|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1669|RAW=At first, the work may be a chamber.
L002513|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1670|RAW=
L002514|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1671|RAW=Then it may become a mirror.
L002515|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1672|RAW=
L002516|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1673|RAW=Then a witness.
L002517|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1674|RAW=
L002518|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1675|RAW=Then a quarry.
L002519|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1676|RAW=
L002520|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1677|RAW=Then a cut stone.
L002521|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1678|RAW=
L002522|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1679|RAW=Then a vessel.
L002523|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1680|RAW=
L002524|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1681|RAW=Then a public object.
L002525|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1682|RAW=
L002526|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1683|RAW=Then a reader’s experience.
L002527|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1684|RAW=
L002528|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1685|RAW=Then a method that returns to the author as craft.
L002529|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1686|RAW=
L002530|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1687|RAW=This matters because the author must not use the same standard for every phase.
L002531|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1688|RAW=
L002532|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1689|RAW=A source draft should not be judged like a finished public piece.
L002533|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1690|RAW=
L002534|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1691|RAW=A self-repair passage should not be forced into reader-facing clarity too early.
L002535|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1692|RAW=
L002536|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1693|RAW=A finished vessel should not keep carrying the whole biography.
L002537|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1694|RAW=
L002538|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1695|RAW=A public piece should not demand that the reader receive the entire source-field before understanding the central contribution.
L002539|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1696|RAW=
L002540|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1697|RAW=## 25.6 Where the rediscovery ends and where it continues
L002541|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1698|RAW=
L002542|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1699|RAW=The rediscovery does not end as living art.
L002543|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1700|RAW=
L002544|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1701|RAW=It should end as identity emergency.
L002545|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1702|RAW=
L002546|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1703|RAW=The author does not stop learning through writing. But the author should eventually stop needing each new work to prove the right to exist, the right to speak, or the right to be understood in total.
L002547|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1704|RAW=
L002548|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1705|RAW=The work matures when writing becomes less like rescue and more like direction.
L002549|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1706|RAW=
L002550|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1707|RAW=The question changes from:
L002551|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1708|RAW=
L002552|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1709|RAW=> Who am I, and how do I explain the whole field so I am not misread?
L002553|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1710|RAW=
L002554|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1711|RAW=To:
L002555|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1712|RAW=
L002556|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1713|RAW=> What is this work, what is its central contribution, and what vessel lets it reach the reader cleanly?
L002557|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1714|RAW=
L002558|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1715|RAW=## 25.7 Practical test: has the work moved from “I” to “it”?
L002559|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1716|RAW=
L002560|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1717|RAW=A piece has moved from “I” to “it” when:
L002561|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1718|RAW=
L002562|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1719|RAW=- it can be cut without feeling like self-betrayal;
L002563|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1720|RAW=- its central contribution can be named in one sentence;
L002564|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1721|RAW=- it can be read by a stranger without the whole biography attached;
L002565|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1722|RAW=- image, structure, rhythm, metaphor, and silence carry some of the meaning;
L002566|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1723|RAW=- the author can ask what the work needs, not only what the self needs;
L002567|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1724|RAW=- the piece can receive editorial pressure without collapsing its living charge;
L002568|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1725|RAW=- the author can preserve the source version without forcing every future version to carry it all;
L002569|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1726|RAW=- the work can become part of a larger body rather than the whole body itself.
L002570|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1727|RAW=
L002571|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1728|RAW=## 25.8 The work’s changing function across the full Source Voice process
L002572|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1729|RAW=
L002573|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1730|RAW=| Developmental function | What the work is doing | Main risk | Correct discipline |
L002574|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1731|RAW=|---|---|---|---|
L002575|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1732|RAW=| Source field | Letting the unmanifested appear | Premature editing | Allow emergence |
L002576|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1733|RAW=| Self-recognition | Showing the author what is actually present | Over-identification | Witness without freezing |
L002577|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1734|RAW=| Identity-repair | Restoring continuity after rupture or silence | Making the piece responsible for saving the self | Let repair happen, then separate |
L002578|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1735|RAW=| Manuscript object | Becoming something that can be shaped | Treating every cut as loss | Move from I to it |
L002579|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1736|RAW=| Editorial vessel | Protecting the reader and the work | Cutting charge instead of congestion | Brutal-sensitive edit |
L002580|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1737|RAW=| Public artifact | Meeting another mind | Over-controlling reception | Make entry clear and leave room |
L002581|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1738|RAW=| Archive/method | Teaching future work | Endless finalizing | Preserve lesson, then move |
L002582|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1739|RAW=
L002583|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1740|RAW=## 25.9 Updated principle for authorship
L002584|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1741|RAW=
L002585|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1742|RAW=The event revealed that editorial was the missing function.
L002586|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1743|RAW=
L002587|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1744|RAW=This later reflection reveals that editorial only works once the author can see which phase the work is in.
L002588|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1745|RAW=
L002589|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1746|RAW=The question is not only:
L002590|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1747|RAW=
L002591|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1748|RAW=> Does this need writing or editing?
L002592|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1749|RAW=
L002593|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1750|RAW=The deeper question is:
L002594|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1751|RAW=
L002595|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1752|RAW=> What face is the work wearing now?
L002596|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1753|RAW=
L002597|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1754|RAW=If it is source, receive it.
L002598|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1755|RAW=
L002599|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1756|RAW=If it is mirror, learn from it.
L002600|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1757|RAW=
L002601|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1758|RAW=If it is repair, let it restore measure.
L002602|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1759|RAW=
L002603|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1760|RAW=If it is object, shape it.
L002604|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1761|RAW=
L002605|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1762|RAW=If it is vessel, protect the reader.
L002606|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1763|RAW=
L002607|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1764|RAW=If it is public, release control of total meaning.
L002608|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1765|RAW=
L002609|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1766|RAW=If it is archive, preserve the lesson and move.
L002610|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1767|RAW=
L002611|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1768|RAW=## 25.10 Updated doctrine
L002612|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1769|RAW=
L002613|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1770|RAW=```text
L002614|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1771|RAW=Write to discover.
L002615|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1772|RAW=Edit to separate.
L002616|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1773|RAW=Shape to transmit.
L002617|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1774|RAW=Share to test.
L002618|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1775|RAW=Return to life to integrate.
L002619|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1776|RAW=Archive the lesson.
L002620|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1777|RAW=Then write again from a clearer level.
L002621|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1778|RAW=```
L002622|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1779|RAW=
L002623|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1780|RAW=One-line addition:
L002624|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1781|RAW=
L002625|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1782|RAW=> **The rediscovery never ends, but it becomes less like rescue and more like mastery.**
L002626|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1783|RAW=
L002627|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1784|RAW=## 25.11 Relation to the two manuscripts
L002628|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1785|RAW=
L002629|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1786|RAW=This applies directly to both major manuscript lines.
L002630|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1787|RAW=
L002631|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1788|RAW=| Manuscript | Early function | Next mature function |
L002632|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1789|RAW=|---|---|---|
L002633|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1790|RAW=| The Measure of Return | Identity-repair, moral proportion, rupture-to-responsibility, continuity restoration. | A shaped testimony / philosophical source manuscript that no longer needs to defend the whole self. |
L002634|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1791|RAW=| The Pre-Form Architecture | Source-field, cosmological pattern, symbolic architecture, unmanifested-to-form language. | A public metaphysical/civilizational vessel that carries the pattern without requiring the full lattice every time. |
L002635|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1792|RAW=
L002636|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1793|RAW=The two works are therefore not only manuscripts.
L002637|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1794|RAW=
L002638|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1795|RAW=They are phase-markers.
L002639|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1796|RAW=
L002640|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1797|RAW=One shows the self returning to measure.
L002641|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1798|RAW=
L002642|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1799|RAW=The other shows source becoming form.
L002643|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1800|RAW=
L002644|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1801|RAW=The author-event lesson now adds the craft bridge:
L002645|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1802|RAW=
L002646|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1803|RAW=> The work must change face before it can reach the reader.
L002647|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1804|RAW=
L002648|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1805|RAW=## 25.12 Future inquiry threads from this addendum
L002649|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1806|RAW=
L002650|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1807|RAW=1. Which current piece is still in I-stage and should not yet be forced into public vessel form?
L002651|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1808|RAW=2. Which piece has already become “it” and is ready for editorial pressure?
L002652|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1809|RAW=3. Which sections are still carrying identity-repair that should remain archived rather than reader-facing?
L002653|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1810|RAW=4. Which sections carry living-art rediscovery and should be preserved as source charge?
L002654|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1811|RAW=5. What is the current face of each manuscript: chamber, mirror, quarry, cut stone, vessel, public object, or method?
L002655|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1812|RAW=6. Where is the author still asking a self-question when the work now needs a craft-question?
L002656|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1813|RAW=7. What would mastery look like if discovery continued but emergency self-definition ended?
L002657|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1814|RAW=8. Which vessel lets the current work serve without needing to rescue the whole self?
L002658|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1815|RAW=
L002659|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1816|RAW=---
L002660|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1817|RAW=
L002661|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1818|RAW=# 26. Additive change log update
L002662|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1819|RAW=
L002663|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1820|RAW=| Version marker | Date | Change |
L002664|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1821|RAW=|---|---:|---|
L002665|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1822|RAW=| 0.1.3-addendum | 2026-04-25 | Added post-event reflection on writing, self-rediscovery, and work-phase transformation. Clarifies that self-rediscovery continues as living art but should stabilize as identity-repair; adds the principle that the work changes face across source, mirror, repair, object, vessel, public artifact, and archive/method phases. Existing sections retained unchanged; this is an additive expansion. |
L002666|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1823|RAW=
L002667|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1824|RAW=---
L002668|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1825|RAW=
L002669|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1826|RAW=# 27. Addendum v0.1.4 — Iteration, Phase Transition, and the Moment the Work Starts Working
L002670|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1827|RAW=
L002671|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1828|RAW=## 27.1 Source reflection added
L002672|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1829|RAW=
L002673|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1830|RAW=A further question arose after the event and after the I-to-it reflection:
L002674|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1831|RAW=
L002675|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1832|RAW=> Why does a piece sometimes not work, not work, not work, and then suddenly work?
L002676|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1833|RAW=
L002677|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1834|RAW=This question names another important layer of the author-event lesson.
L002678|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1835|RAW=
L002679|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1836|RAW=The event revealed that **editorial** was the missing function. The later I-to-it reflection revealed that the work changes face as it moves from source, mirror, repair chamber, manuscript object, editorial vessel, public artifact, and archive/method.
L002680|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1837|RAW=
L002681|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1838|RAW=This reflection adds a third layer:
L002682|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1839|RAW=
L002683|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1840|RAW=> A piece does not usually begin working because one sentence was finally improved. It begins working because enough hidden conditions have converged for the life of the work to become visible.
L002684|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1841|RAW=
L002685|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1842|RAW=The working moment may feel sudden, but the suddenness is usually only the moment of recognition.
L002686|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1843|RAW=
L002687|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1844|RAW=The work has been gathering its conditions underneath the surface.
L002688|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1845|RAW=
L002689|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1846|RAW=## 27.2 Core discovery
L002690|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1847|RAW=
L002691|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1848|RAW=The repeated failure of a piece is not always a sign that the piece is wrong.
L002692|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1849|RAW=
L002693|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1850|RAW=Sometimes it means the piece is still missing one of its governing conditions:
L002694|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1851|RAW=
L002695|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1852|RAW=- its central contribution has not been named;
L002696|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1853|RAW=- the wrong vessel is carrying the charge;
L002697|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1854|RAW=- too much meaning is still forced through explanation;
L002698|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1855|RAW=- the image-system has not begun doing its share of the work;
L002699|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1856|RAW=- the author is still fused with the piece at I-stage;
L002700|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1857|RAW=- the reader door has not appeared;
L002701|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1858|RAW=- the piece has not yet found its chairing question;
L002702|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1859|RAW=- the cut has not removed congestion;
L002703|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1860|RAW=- the form-pressure is too weak or too tight;
L002704|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1861|RAW=- the work has not yet become separate enough to be shaped.
L002705|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1862|RAW=
L002706|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1863|RAW=The piece may therefore appear to be failing when it is actually clarifying the conditions it needs.
L002707|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1864|RAW=
L002708|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1865|RAW=## 27.3 The phase-transition model
L002709|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1866|RAW=
L002710|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1867|RAW=Creative work often changes through **phase transition**, not linear improvement.
L002711|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1868|RAW=
L002712|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1869|RAW=A liquid does not become steam by improving one molecule at a time in a way the eye can easily see. Heat accumulates. Conditions change. Then, at a threshold, the state changes.
L002713|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1870|RAW=
L002714|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1871|RAW=Writing can behave like that.
L002715|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1872|RAW=
L002716|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1873|RAW=A manuscript may receive several passes that appear not to solve it. One pass clarifies the image. One pass reveals the governing metaphor. One pass exposes the false opening. One pass shows the piece is still too close to the self. One pass identifies the reader. One pass cuts the wrong section. One pass discovers that the essay should be a prose-poem, or that the poem should be a source note, or that the source note should be a public talk.
L002717|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1874|RAW=
L002718|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1875|RAW=Then the next pass appears to make the whole piece work.
L002719|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1876|RAW=
L002720|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1877|RAW=But that pass was not alone.
L002721|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1878|RAW=
L002722|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1879|RAW=It was the threshold where previous invisible work became visible.
L002723|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1880|RAW=
L002724|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1881|RAW=## 27.4 Core mechanism
L002725|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1882|RAW=
L002726|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1883|RAW=```text
L002727|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1884|RAW=Repeated iteration
L002728|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1885|RAW=→ hidden variables align
L002729|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1886|RAW=→ carrier overload resolves
L002730|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1887|RAW=→ work separates from self
L002731|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1888|RAW=→ vessel fits charge
L002732|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1889|RAW=→ reader door appears
L002733|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1890|RAW=→ the piece suddenly works
L002734|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1891|RAW=```
L002735|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1892|RAW=
L002736|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1893|RAW=Or, more simply:
L002737|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1894|RAW=
L002738|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1895|RAW=> The work works when the form finally becomes equal to the charge.
L002739|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1896|RAW=
L002740|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1897|RAW=## 27.5 What “not working” actually means
L002741|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1898|RAW=
L002742|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1899|RAW=When a piece does not work, the surface diagnosis is often inaccurate.
L002743|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1900|RAW=
L002744|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1901|RAW=The author may think:
L002745|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1902|RAW=
L002746|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1903|RAW=> The language is not good enough.
L002747|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1904|RAW=
L002748|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1905|RAW=But the deeper condition may be different.
L002749|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1906|RAW=
L002750|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1907|RAW=| Apparent problem | Deeper condition | Required pass |
L002751|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1908|RAW=|---|---|---|
L002752|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1909|RAW=| The language feels heavy | Too much meaning is being carried by explanation | Carrier reassignment pass |
L002753|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1910|RAW=| The piece feels flat | The image-system has not started carrying charge | Image/metaphor pass |
L002754|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1911|RAW=| The piece feels scattered | The chairing question is missing | Governing-question pass |
L002755|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1912|RAW=| The piece feels too private | It is still in I-stage rather than it-stage | Separation pass |
L002756|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1913|RAW=| The piece feels overbuilt | The vessel is too large or too architectural | Vessel-reduction pass |
L002757|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1914|RAW=| The piece feels thin | The vessel is too small for the charge | Expansion or grounding pass |
L002758|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1915|RAW=| The piece does not land | The reader door has not appeared | Reader-entry pass |
L002759|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1916|RAW=| The piece repeats itself | The same meaning is not being advanced through new carriers | Deduplication / progression pass |
L002760|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1917|RAW=| The piece feels clever but dead | Craft is present but living charge has been over-cut | Re-source pass |
L002761|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1918|RAW=| The piece feels alive but unreadable | Source is present but editorial has not protected the reader | Brutal-sensitive edit |
L002762|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1919|RAW=
L002763|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1920|RAW=The lesson is that “not working” is not one diagnosis.
L002764|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1921|RAW=
L002765|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1922|RAW=It is a signal to identify which hidden condition is missing.
L002766|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1923|RAW=
L002767|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1924|RAW=## 27.6 Iteration as condition-building
L002768|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1925|RAW=
L002769|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1926|RAW=Iteration should not be judged only by visible success.
L002770|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1927|RAW=
L002771|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1928|RAW=A pass can be valuable even if the piece still does not yet work.
L002772|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1929|RAW=
L002773|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1930|RAW=| Pass type | Hidden condition clarified |
L002774|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1931|RAW=|---|---|
L002775|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1932|RAW=| Source pass | What is trying to come through |
L002776|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1933|RAW=| Essence pass | What the piece is actually giving |
L002777|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1934|RAW=| Image pass | What carries the charge without explanation |
L002778|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1935|RAW=| Theme pass | What repeats and therefore governs |
L002779|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1936|RAW=| Vessel pass | What form can hold the material |
L002780|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1937|RAW=| Cut pass | What blocks entry or breath |
L002781|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1938|RAW=| I-to-it pass | What belongs to self-recovery versus the work-object |
L002782|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1939|RAW=| Reader pass | Where a stranger can enter |
L002783|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1940|RAW=| Silence pass | What does not need to be said |
L002784|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1941|RAW=| Archive pass | What must be preserved elsewhere so the current piece can be free |
L002785|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1942|RAW=
L002786|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1943|RAW=The failed-looking version may still have performed one essential function.
L002787|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1944|RAW=
L002788|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1945|RAW=It may have taught what the final version no longer needs to carry.
L002789|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1946|RAW=
L002790|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1947|RAW=## 27.7 The “click”
L002791|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1948|RAW=
L002792|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1949|RAW=The click happens when enough of the following conditions converge:
L002793|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1950|RAW=
L002794|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1951|RAW=- the central contribution can be named;
L002795|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1952|RAW=- the correct vessel is chosen;
L002796|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1953|RAW=- the strongest image begins carrying more than explanation;
L002797|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1954|RAW=- the theme is governing rather than merely appearing;
L002798|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1955|RAW=- the author can cut without self-betrayal;
L002799|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1956|RAW=- the reader has an entry point;
L002800|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1957|RAW=- the piece has enough form-pressure to concentrate the charge;
L002801|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1958|RAW=- the work is no longer trying to be the whole field;
L002802|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1959|RAW=- the piece has become “it” enough to receive editorial pressure;
L002803|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1960|RAW=- the silence around the language is doing some of the work.
L002804|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1961|RAW=
L002805|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1962|RAW=At that point, the piece begins to feel inevitable.
L002806|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1963|RAW=
L002807|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1964|RAW=It no longer feels like material being pushed into a shape.
L002808|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1965|RAW=
L002809|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1966|RAW=It feels like the shape the material was waiting for.
L002810|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1967|RAW=
L002811|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1968|RAW=## 27.8 Relation to Source Voice
L002812|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1969|RAW=
L002813|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1970|RAW=This discovery is central to Source Voice because Source Voice often begins as more field than form.
L002814|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1971|RAW=
L002815|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1972|RAW=The first appearance of the material may be too large, too alive, too charged, too interwoven, or too personally fused to become reader-facing immediately.
L002816|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1973|RAW=
L002817|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1974|RAW=That does not mean the Source Voice is wrong.
L002818|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1975|RAW=
L002819|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1976|RAW=It means Source Voice requires a sequence:
L002820|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1977|RAW=
L002821|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1978|RAW=```text
L002822|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1979|RAW=source field
L002823|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1980|RAW=→ first capture
L002824|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1981|RAW=→ self-recognition
L002825|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1982|RAW=→ central contribution
L002826|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1983|RAW=→ carrier assignment
L002827|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1984|RAW=→ vessel selection
L002828|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1985|RAW=→ editorial cut
L002829|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1986|RAW=→ reader door
L002830|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1987|RAW=→ public or private form
L002831|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1988|RAW=```
L002832|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1989|RAW=
L002833|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1990|RAW=The voice is not only the raw arrival.
L002834|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1991|RAW=
L002835|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1992|RAW=The mature voice includes the ability to recognize what phase the work is in and which condition must be built next.
L002836|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1993|RAW=
L002837|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1994|RAW=## 27.9 Relation to the event lesson
L002838|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1995|RAW=
L002839|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1996|RAW=The event taught that a piece carrying a lot of meaning must distribute meaning across words, structure, image, theme, metaphor, silence, rhythm, and reader participation.
L002840|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1997|RAW=
L002841|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1998|RAW=This addendum explains why that distribution may not happen immediately.
L002842|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=1999|RAW=
L002843|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2000|RAW=The author may need several iterations before discovering which carrier should hold which layer.
L002844|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2001|RAW=
L002845|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2002|RAW=A draft may be failing because language is trying to do the work of image.
L002846|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2003|RAW=
L002847|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2004|RAW=Another may fail because structure is trying to do the work of theme.
L002848|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2005|RAW=
L002849|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2006|RAW=Another may fail because the author is trying to control reader interpretation through over-explanation.
L002850|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2007|RAW=
L002851|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2008|RAW=Another may fail because the living charge has not yet been separated from the personal urgency that first brought it forward.
L002852|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2009|RAW=
L002853|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2010|RAW=The editorial task is therefore diagnostic:
L002854|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2011|RAW=
L002855|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2012|RAW=> Do not only ask whether the piece works. Ask which carrier is overloaded and which condition has not yet appeared.
L002856|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2013|RAW=
L002857|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2014|RAW=## 27.10 Relation to the I-to-it movement
L002858|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2015|RAW=
L002859|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2016|RAW=The piece often cannot fully work while it is still identical to the author.
L002860|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2017|RAW=
L002861|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2018|RAW=In I-stage, the work may be too protective, too explanatory, too total, too defensive, too private, or too burdened by identity-continuity.
L002862|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2019|RAW=
L002863|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2020|RAW=This does not make I-stage wrong.
L002864|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2021|RAW=
L002865|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2022|RAW=I-stage may be necessary for discovery.
L002866|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2023|RAW=
L002867|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2024|RAW=But the click usually requires at least partial movement into it-stage.
L002868|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2025|RAW=
L002869|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2026|RAW=Only then can the author ask:
L002870|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2027|RAW=
L002871|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2028|RAW=- What does the piece need?
L002872|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2029|RAW=- What is the piece not?
L002873|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2030|RAW=- What can be cut?
L002874|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2031|RAW=- What belongs in archive rather than front-end?
L002875|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2032|RAW=- What should the reader receive first?
L002876|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2033|RAW=- What image should carry what explanation currently carries?
L002877|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2034|RAW=
L002878|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2035|RAW=The work starts working when it becomes separate enough to be served.
L002879|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2036|RAW=
L002880|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2037|RAW=## 27.11 Relation to the two manuscripts
L002881|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2038|RAW=
L002882|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2039|RAW=This applies directly to both major manuscripts.
L002883|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2040|RAW=
L002884|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2041|RAW=| Manuscript | Why it may not work in early versions | What makes it begin to work |
L002885|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2042|RAW=|---|---|---|
L002886|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2043|RAW=| The Pre-Form Architecture | Too much cosmology, governance, Giza, aether, language, technology, and civilization trying to appear at once. | The source line becomes clear: form must remember source. Giza becomes interface. Capstone becomes responsibility. The rest can distribute into sections, images, or later works. |
L002887|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2044|RAW=| The Measure of Return | Too much rupture, explanation, moral accounting, identity-repair, substrate, and self-rule trying to prove the whole life at once. | The central line becomes clear: return is responsibility finally given form. The piece can become testimony and method rather than total defense. |
L002888|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2045|RAW=
L002889|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2046|RAW=The large versions are not failures.
L002890|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2047|RAW=
L002891|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2048|RAW=They are condition-builders.
L002892|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2049|RAW=
L002893|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2050|RAW=They contain the quarry, the archive, the overgrowth, the hidden images, the living charge, and the excess that reveals the real center by contrast.
L002894|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2051|RAW=
L002895|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2052|RAW=The compressed versions work when they stop trying to carry the entire field and instead carry the governing essence.
L002896|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2053|RAW=
L002897|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2054|RAW=## 27.12 How to use this discovery in practice
L002898|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2055|RAW=
L002899|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2056|RAW=When a piece is not working, do not immediately rewrite everything.
L002900|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2057|RAW=
L002901|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2058|RAW=Ask:
L002902|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2059|RAW=
L002903|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2060|RAW=1. Is the central contribution clear?
L002904|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2061|RAW=2. Is the vessel correct?
L002905|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2062|RAW=3. Is too much meaning being carried by direct explanation?
L002906|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2063|RAW=4. What image wants to carry more?
L002907|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2064|RAW=5. What structure can carry instead of another paragraph?
L002908|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2065|RAW=6. What should be silent?
L002909|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2066|RAW=7. What belongs in archive?
L002910|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2067|RAW=8. Is the piece still I, or has it become it?
L002911|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2068|RAW=9. Where does the reader enter?
L002912|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2069|RAW=10. What hidden condition did this failed version clarify?
L002913|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2070|RAW=
L002914|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2071|RAW=Then choose one pass.
L002915|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2072|RAW=
L002916|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2073|RAW=Do not make every pass do every kind of work.
L002917|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2074|RAW=
L002918|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2075|RAW=## 27.13 Editorial implication
L002919|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2076|RAW=
L002920|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2077|RAW=The editor is not only a cutter.
L002921|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2078|RAW=
L002922|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2079|RAW=The editor is a condition-reader.
L002923|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2080|RAW=
L002924|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2081|RAW=The editor asks:
L002925|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2082|RAW=
L002926|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2083|RAW=- What phase is this work in?
L002927|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2084|RAW=- Which condition is missing?
L002928|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2085|RAW=- Which carrier is overloaded?
L002929|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2086|RAW=- Which part is alive but misplaced?
L002930|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2087|RAW=- Which section belongs in archive?
L002931|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2088|RAW=- Which image should be trusted?
L002932|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2089|RAW=- Which silence would let the reader participate?
L002933|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2090|RAW=- Which cut would let the truth travel?
L002934|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2091|RAW=
L002935|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2092|RAW=This makes editorial less like judgment and more like midwifery.
L002936|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2093|RAW=
L002937|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2094|RAW=The editor does not decide whether the source deserves to exist.
L002938|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2095|RAW=
L002939|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2096|RAW=The editor helps the source find the form in which it can live.
L002940|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2097|RAW=
L002941|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2098|RAW=## 27.14 Governing principle
L002942|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2099|RAW=
L002943|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2100|RAW=> Iteration is not only improvement.  
L002944|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2101|RAW=> Iteration is condition-building.  
L002945|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2102|RAW=> A piece starts working when enough hidden conditions converge.
L002946|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2103|RAW=
L002947|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2104|RAW=## 27.15 Updated doctrine
L002948|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2105|RAW=
L002949|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2106|RAW=```text
L002950|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2107|RAW=Do not judge every iteration by visible success.
L002951|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2108|RAW=Ask which hidden condition it clarified.
L002952|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2109|RAW=One pass may find the essence.
L002953|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2110|RAW=One pass may find the image.
L002954|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2111|RAW=One pass may find the cut.
L002955|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2112|RAW=One pass may find the vessel.
L002956|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2113|RAW=One pass may find the reader door.
L002957|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2114|RAW=The work works when these are finally in relation.
L002958|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2115|RAW=```
L002959|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2116|RAW=
L002960|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2117|RAW=One-line addition:
L002961|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2118|RAW=
L002962|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2119|RAW=> **The work does not suddenly start working; the hidden structure finally becomes visible.**
L002963|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2120|RAW=
L002964|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2121|RAW=## 27.16 Future inquiry threads from this addendum
L002965|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2122|RAW=
L002966|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2123|RAW=1. Which current piece appears not to work because its vessel is wrong?
L002967|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2124|RAW=2. Which piece has source charge but no reader door?
L002968|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2125|RAW=3. Which piece has a strong image that is not yet being trusted enough?
L002969|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2126|RAW=4. Which piece is still asking language to carry what structure, metaphor, rhythm, or silence should carry?
L002970|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2127|RAW=5. Which failed draft clarified a hidden condition even though it did not become final?
L002971|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2128|RAW=6. Which manuscript has reached the click, and what conditions converged to make it work?
L002972|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2129|RAW=7. Which manuscript still needs phase transition rather than more line-editing?
L002973|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2130|RAW=8. How can the editorial process record what each iteration discovered, not only whether it succeeded?
L002974|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2131|RAW=9. What is the smallest visible change that would reveal the hidden structure already present?
L002975|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2132|RAW=10. Which version should be archived as quarry rather than judged as failure?
L002976|SOURCE_LINE|SOURCE_ID=SRC02|ORIGINAL_LINE=2133|RAW=
